Important News 2

The Situation of Both Sides After the End of the War in Fujian 57

Commander Lu Still Plans a Counterattack from the West Route

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since Commander Liu He-ding completely defeated Commander Lu Xing-bang's troops in the northwestern suburbs of Fuzhou on the morning of the 13th, there are no enemy traces on the northern route. Commander Lu's troops on the western route have retreated to Baisha, eighty li from the provincial capital, but it is still reported that two regiments will be transferred from Yanping Shuikou to Commander Lu's troops, preparing for a counterattack. Commander Liu's troops have only advanced to Tongkou, thirty li from the provincial capital. However, the key passes of Ma'anshan Dafuling on the northern route and Baishalun Wanshoushan on the western route are still guarded by about two regiments of troops, and the defenses are very strict. In the Nangang area, after Commander Lu's troops retreated into Yongtai County, they contacted local bandits Wu Da-ang and Huang Qi-lan, and fought fiercely with the two units of the provincial police team, Liang Ji-chuan and Huang Bing-wu. The fighting has not stopped for three days. Liang and Huang telegraphed the province the day before yesterday to request that troops be sent to assist them. In addition, Liu He-ding hosted a banquet at Hanyuan outside the Shuibu Gate a few days ago, inviting members of the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, the General Chamber of Commerce, and the General Federation of Trade Unions to express his gratitude for their support this time. Yesterday, he hosted a banquet at the division headquarters to entertain the regimental, battalion, and company commanders who participated in the battle, to reward their achievements. At the same time, the Special Party Department printed various leaflets advising Commander Lu's troops and handed them to the naval seaplane Haiyan to distribute them to Baisha Shuikou, urging them to become enlightened. According to a conversation with a military officer of Commander Liu's troops, based on the experience of this battle, although Commander Lu's troops have many soldiers, they lack training; although they have enough weapons, they are not sophisticated. Therefore, there is not much concern about the counterattack, and so on.

Regarding news about Commander Lu's troops, it is rumored that this battle was entirely presided over by Lu Xing-rong, the commander of the Fifth Brigade, and Yang Yu-gu, the chief staff officer of the division headquarters. Lu Xing-bang himself and Lu Xing-ming, the commander of the Fourth Brigade, did not have any preconceived ideas. Therefore, the soldiers fighting were all troops under the jurisdiction of Lu Xing-rong. After this defeat, internal opinions were quite inconsistent. The Minqing faction (Commander Lu's troops are divided into three factions internally, with most of the strategists being from the Fuzhou faction, and the strongmen being divided into the Minqing and Youxi factions) is quite close to southern Fujian due to their hometown relationship with Xu Xian-shi (i.e., the arrested provincial committee member) and Huang Bing-wu, and mostly advocate peace talks. The Fuzhou faction mostly advocates fighting again in order to enter the provincial capital. The Youxi faction advocates shortening the defense line and retreating to Shuikou, temporarily severing relations with the province to wait and see what happens. Observing the trends in Commander Lu's actions in recent days, it is possible that they will follow the Youxi faction's proposal. However, since the outbreak of the war, the province's financial resources have gradually become strained because Commander Lu's troops have intercepted taxes from more than 20 counties in northern Fujian. In terms of commerce, the export of large quantities of paper, wood, bamboo, tea, bamboo shoots, and charcoal, all of which come from upstream, has been cut off, and it has also been suspended. Therefore, the scourge of war has had a particularly significant impact on commerce. (June 19)

Qingdao

Trouble at the Minghua Bank 58

Caused by Rumors Spread by the Japanese

Qingdao Correspondence: The Minghua Savings Bank on Zhongshan Road in this city has a solid foundation and its business is divided into three departments: commercial, savings, and trust. The bank has about 3,000 depositors and deposits of about 2 million yuan. It has always had a good reputation and annual profits. This time, due to rumors spread by the Japanese, a run on the bank occurred yesterday (the 18th). Today, many depositors are still crowding to withdraw their deposits. The Public Security Bureau, fearing disturbances, has dispatched dozens of police officers to maintain order at the front and back doors of the bank. Anyone who withdraws money must first obtain a number from the nearby police station and enter to withdraw money according to the number. Therefore, the order is still not chaotic. The banking community and the General Chamber of Commerce of this city held an emergency meeting last night to maintain the market and discuss maintenance measures, and selected personnel to go to the bank to check the accounts. The results of the investigation showed that there were no deficits and tens of thousands of yuan in surplus. However, because the bank has handled trusts and has dozens of real estate properties, the existing cash is not enough to cope with the situation. The banks decided that from the 19th, they would provide 200,000 yuan per day, including 60,000 yuan from the Bank of China, 60,000 yuan from the Bank of Communications, 40,000 yuan from the Shanzuo Bank, and 20,000 yuan each from the Dalu Bank and the Zhonglu Bank. In addition to the above funds, the bank also remitted a large amount of cash from Shanghai to provide assistance. It is estimated that about 200,000 yuan was withdrawn on the 18th and more than 600,000 yuan was withdrawn today (the 19th). The bank still has a lot of deposits and can cope with the situation without being affected. The municipal government also issued a notice today to refute the rumors for the bank. The notice is as follows: "According to reports, on the 18th of this month, depositors of the Minghua Bank in this city have been withdrawing their deposits one after another, and there have been some disturbances. The reason for the investigation is that there are rumors that the Shanghai head office has gone bankrupt, causing panic. The bank has been established in this city for a long time and has a good reputation. Its Shanghai head office has no unstable news. Depositors can fully trust the bank and not believe rumors, so as not to cause disturbances." (June 19)

Liaoning Destroys Heroin for the Second Time by Burning 59

Shenyang Correspondence: A large batch of heroin, totaling 239 packages, was seized by the postal bureau from Germany via Siberia to a Japanese person in Changchun. Together with a package of heroin seized earlier from Switzerland, it was publicly destroyed by the provincial government in Xiaohaiyan Public Stadium on the 16th in accordance with the scheduled method. The heroin sent from Germany this time is worth about one million yuan in total. In order to deceive people, the traffickers dyed it in various colors such as red, blue, pink, brown, and yellow to pretend to be dyes. Each box weighs about twenty taels, and is packed in a tin box of about three inches square with a round lid. On the lid is a white round piece of paper with different words. The outer packaging is a yellow paper box, and the cover is thick yellow paper with a square of white paper pasted on it, printed with the address of the package, etc. In addition, there is a package of heroin (white) previously sent from Switzerland, which is contained in a flat and long iron box, weighing about two pounds. It was previously sent to Yingkou for chemical inspection and was destroyed together this time. On that day, two mat sheds were set up in the stadium, and pictures, slogans, charts, etc. of the Anti-Drug Association were pasted inside and outside. The central one was used for inspection and unpacking, and the north one was used for entertaining guests. Before 11:00 a.m., representatives of various agencies arrived one after another. Foreigners included consuls from Britain, France, Germany, Austria, and the Soviet Union, as well as Baltic, the Liaoning Postmaster, Xiao, the Customs Commissioner, and others. At about 11:20 a.m., all the heroin was transported by car and immediately followed the previous procedure, first inspecting the cover, then opening the package and retaining samples (half a spoonful was taken from each box and placed in an envelope, and each envelope was sealed with sealing wax and signed by Yan Yu-heng for preservation). It was not until about 1:00 p.m. that all 240 packages were opened. Because the square box with a round opening was not easy to empty, it was placed together with the tin box in the prepared four large pots, and kerosene was used to light the firewood up and down. The stove built with bricks was lit, and black waves rose up. All the visitors left their seats and hurriedly avoided the wind to avoid poisoning. The photography and filming activities of the Cultural Society and the Guangming Photography Studio were very busy. After a while, the smoke and fire gradually subsided, and it was gradually burned completely. All the people who came to the stadium then dispersed one after another. (June 16)

Harbin City to Build a Waterworks 60

The Harbin City Council Ordered to Reorganize

Harbin Correspondence: The Harbin City waterworks construction plan has been going on for three years. The authorities, in view of the failure of the Jilin waterworks construction, are extremely cautious in order to avoid wasting huge sums of money and achieving no results. First, a waterworks construction committee was established in the Special City Bureau the year before last, with specialized personnel from the Governor's Office, the Special City Council, the City Bureau, and other agencies responsible for the design. Recently, it was learned that the waterworks in Tianjin, Beiping, Hankou, and other ports are all old-style constructions, and there is no need to imitate them. Only the Zhabei waterworks in Shanghai is a new-style construction. Therefore, it was decided to send technicians to inspect it immediately, so as to learn from it. When construction begins in the future, bidding will be invited in batches. Items such as machines and water pipes will be contracted separately to avoid being deceived by intermediaries. Bidding will begin on July 1, and construction is expected to begin in the middle of August. The city is divided into five districts, starting with Daoli, and then extending to Daowai, Majiagou, Xiangfang, and Bazhan. It is expected to be completed in two years. The construction cost is set at 3 million yuan. It has been decided to issue municipal bonds worth 2 million yuan in late July, specifically for this project. As for the city's improvement of sewers, four-fifths have been completed, and it will be completed by the end of next month. While the city's construction is underway, the city council suddenly heard of reorganization. The reason is that the Harbin City Council was established after it was recovered in 1926. The charter was drafted, imitating Pingjin, and incorporating the board of directors situation of the old British and Russian agreements. The Municipal Bureau, the executive agency, has one officially appointed mayor and one assistant officer each. The other assistant officer and two section chiefs are recommended by the citizens and appointed by the government. The opinions of the officially appointed and citizen-recommended parties are often in opposite positions, resulting in occasional disputes. At the same time, the number of city self-government councilors is as high as 40. At each meeting, there are many people and mixed opinions, which often leads to disputes. As a result, the Municipal Bureau, the executive agency, often does not know what to do. In the newly elected third session of city councilors this year, there are some who were illegally elected, resulting in lawsuits in court. The supervisory agency cannot handle it. The current mayor, He Yu-fang, specially reported it to the Northeast Road Committee, which ordered the Administrative Governor's Office to reorganize the city council, abolish the third session of councilors, and conduct elections. The city's organizational charter and the systems of assistant officers and councilors will be revised. The election will be held around next month, and the new council will be convened around September. Before the new council is convened, all construction in the city will be submitted to the Administrative Governor's Office for approval and implementation, and will be sent to the City Council for retroactive approval in the future to comply with the procedures. (June 15)

The Ministry of Agriculture and Mining's Views on Relief for the Unemployed 61

(Continued)

C. Matters Concerning the Mining Industry

(1) Maintaining Shutdown Coal Mines (Reasons) China's coal industry is roughly divided into foreign-funded and state-owned. In 1928, the output of foreign-funded coal mines was about 13 million tons. Calculated at a coal production rate of 0.450 per worker, a total of about 80,000 miners were employed. The output of state-owned coal mines was about 12 million tons. Calculated at a coal production rate of 0.210 per worker, a total of 157,000 miners were needed. This means that the output of state-owned coal mines is less than half that of foreign-funded coal mines, while the number of workers is twice as high. This is because there are fewer machine plants and more native kilns. In addition, the main foreign-funded mines, such as the Fushun and Kailuan mines, are all located in the northeastern provinces, where the area is relatively peaceful and there is foreign protection, so they can develop in an orderly manner. State-owned mines are mostly located in the interior of China and are subject to military, bandit, communist, and transportation influences, which have led to the decline of the mining industry. In the past one or two years, coal mines near the Pinghan, Jinpu, and Jiaoji railways have been shut down one after another due to inconvenient transportation or disturbances by soldiers and bandits. Coal mines in Jiangxi and Hunan have also ceased operations. If the number of workers in state-owned coal mines in 1928 is calculated with 70% unemployed, it has reached 110,000 people. If we want to relieve these unemployed workers, maintaining state-owned coal mines is the first priority. (Measures) 1. The government should prepare 3 million yuan to subsidize or lend to various coal mining companies to supervise and order them to start work as soon as possible. 2. A special allocation of 800,000 yuan should be made to the Pingxiang Coal Mine, which will be temporarily maintained by the government. 3. The Ministry of Railways should be ordered to increase the number of vehicles on each route as soon as possible, reduce freight rates, and eliminate loopholes to facilitate transportation.

(2) Reorganizing Gold Mines in the Eastern Provinces (Reasons) Most of China's gold production comes from placer gold mines, and the most prosperous placer gold mines are in the northeast, with Heilongjiang being the first and Jilin being the second. For example, in Duoku, Mohe, Qiqian River, Yuqinggou, and Yilan Huachuan, the government used to set up bureaus to mine gold, and the output was very high. After 1916, due to the impact of the European War, silver rose and gold fell, and mining could not make a profit, so the mining industry was suspended, and the number of unemployed reached tens of thousands. Although there are more than 30 gold mining companies that continue to mine, most of them are speculative in nature. The capital is not sufficient, and the technology is not good enough. It is difficult to develop by digging here and there, and the remaining tens of thousands of workers have no hope of resuming their careers. We should find ways to restore the gold mining industry in the area to relieve the unemployed workers. ) (Measures) The government should allocate 1 million yuan to temporarily establish gold mining bureaus in Heihe and Shiwei in Heilongjiang and Yilan in Jilin, recruit workers to select sites for mining, and plan for development. (3) Reorganizing Tungsten Mines in Southern Jiangxi (Reasons) The most abundant tungsten mines in China are in the counties of southern Jiangxi, followed by Hunan and Guangxi. In 1928, the national output of tungsten sand was more than 7,300 tons, worth about 2.5 million yuan, accounting for 60% of the world's output. The output of Jiangxi province alone accounts for 90% of the national output. Therefore, tens of thousands of people in southern Jiangxi rely on mining tungsten sand for a living. In the past, merchants organized companies to contract for collection and sales. Now this company has been expressly ordered to be abolished. The government should run it itself to maintain the livelihood of tens of thousands of unemployed people. (Measures) The central government and the Jiangxi provincial government should jointly raise 1 million yuan to establish a bureau to recruit workers for mining, temporarily using the sand collection method, while purchasing machinery for large-scale equipment.

(4) Restoring Mercury Mines in Guizhou (Reasons) China's mercury ore is mostly produced in Guizhou, such as the counties of Shengxi, Tongren, Bazhai, Zijiang, Xiuwen, Nanlong, and Qianxi. Shengxi and Bazhai are the most famous. Others, such as Fenghuang in Hunan and Youyang in Sichuan, are also known for producing mercury. In the past, the mercury ore production of Guizhou province alone reached 1,000 tons per year. During the European War, in addition to domestic use, the export of mercury reached 200 tons per year. Since then, the local area has been unstable, and mining and transportation have been difficult. The mining industry in various places has therefore declined. A few years ago, there was still a small amount of production, but now it has been completely stopped. As a result, all the raw sand silver used in the country relies on foreign countries, and the annual losses are very large. The unemployed miners in these provinces, about tens of thousands, are very worrying. (Measures) The government should temporarily allocate 200,000 yuan to establish bureaus for mining and transportation in Tongren and Huangping counties in Guizhou to make adjustments and seek development.

The above four measures concerning the mining industry are based on the actual situation and are urgent and feasible. A total of 6 million yuan is needed, and about 300,000 unemployed miners can be relieved. In addition, undeveloped coal and iron mines, copper mines in Yunnan, oil mines in Shaanxi and Gansu, and iron plants in Hanyelongyan are difficult to implement due to inconvenient transportation, high costs, or excessive expenses. They will be planned separately, so they will not be listed. (The End)

Wuxi 66

The Sericulture Suppression Office Dispatches Personnel to Supervise Various Districts: The Sericulture Suppression Office of the Department of Agriculture and Mining previously dispatched personnel to various breeding grounds three times during the spring silkworm breeding season to earnestly supervise. It then submitted a report to the Department of Agriculture and Mining regarding the Huinong and other eight breeding farms, which were found to have substandard breeding practices. Locust Nymphs Appear in Farmland Near the Lake: Yesterday, the county government received a report from Zhu Yu, the district head of the Fourth District (Kaiyuan Township), stating that reeds grow luxuriantly along Taihu Lake, north of Mount Hui. After continuous plum rains, countless locust nymphs suddenly appeared, damaging eighty to ninety mu of nearby fertile land. The seedlings have been completely destroyed. Furthermore, an investigation revealed that the entire area along the lake is infested. Upon receiving the report, County Magistrate Sun immediately ordered the district to supervise the villagers in quickly capturing and exterminating the locusts, setting a price for them, and having the district office purchase them. Simultaneously, the county submitted a report to the Department of Agriculture and Mining for verification.

Various Parties Deliberate on Adjusting the Rice Shortage: The price of rice in Wuxi is soaring, and the rice reserves are dwindling daily. Various parties are devising ways to prepare for relief. Tang Weizhi sent a letter to various sectors a few days ago, advocating for the rapid organization of a relief association and hoping that farmers' banks in various places would emulate social methods of purchasing rice and lending it to farmers. However, Gu Shuzhi, the director of the Fourth District Office of the Provincial Farmers' Bank, stated that the Wuxi Farmers' Bank was newly established and is currently actively preparing for agricultural credit lending. However, its funds are limited, making it difficult to purchase rice and lend it to the people. Various districts are currently preparing for price controls and will provide assistance to the best of their ability. The Millstone Industry Association also held an urgent temporary meeting yesterday to vigorously seek ways to adjust the situation. It was decided to send a letter to the Joint Association of Rice Industry Associations of Shanghai, Jiangsu Province, and the Ninghu Municipal and County, informing the rice industry in both the north and south that imported foreign rice should first be circulated in the province's interior to alleviate the people's hardships. At the same time, a request was submitted to the county government to expedite price controls to temporarily maintain the current situation.

County Government Interrogates Extortion Suspects at Night: The case of Miao Picheng, the former director of the Department of Civil Affairs, being repeatedly threatened by bandits has caused widespread discussion. Qian Tianxiong, the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, led police officers to successively arrest three main suspects in this case, Deng Asan, Lü Yulian, and Hang Bingkui, in Badou Lane outside the North Gate and in Jiuchengli in Xicun. They were handed over to the county for interrogation the day before yesterday. Yesterday late at night, County Magistrate Sun Zuji personally conducted the interrogation, prohibiting bystanders from listening, so the details of the testimony are unknown. However, it was heard that the testimonies of Lü and Hang were largely the same as their testimonies at the Public Security Bureau, while Deng was still being evasive. As a result, County Magistrate Sun ordered all of them to be shackled and sent to prison to await further interrogation and judgment.

Yang Zhongtian Sued Again: Yang Zhongtian, from Yangtie Lane, Yangming Township, Wuxi County, was originally a vagrant. Later, he became a silk cocoon broker and now operates the Wanfeng Silk Cocoon Company along the river at the Labor Movement Bridge. In recent years, he has also been heavily involved in the silkworm egg trade, making substantial profits. As a result, Yang is in a very wealthy situation and spends his days gambling and smoking opium. Last year, he was sued once for selling inferior silkworm eggs. Recently, Yang Zhongtian was accused of attempting to default on more than a thousand yuan in dried cocoon payments. Nineteen cocoon households, including Shao Sisheng, Yu Ruzhou, and Zhang Maoqing, jointly filed a civil lawsuit with the county government to pursue the debt. The day before yesterday, the households took Yang into custody and collectively interrogated him. Zhou, the trial officer, opened a court to conduct the trial. Yang claimed that the debt had already been paid. Zhou asked why, if the debt had been paid, he did not collect and cancel the joint receipt, allowing others to keep it. At this point, Yang had no response. After the interrogation, he was ordered to post bail and await further summons.

Wuxi Suffers Calamities from Plum Rains: Since the beginning of the plum rain season in this county, there have been continuous heavy rains, and the river water has risen sharply to more than two chi. The city streets are flooded, making it difficult for pedestrians to travel. Farmers in the surrounding countryside are currently transplanting rice seedlings. These plum rains have slightly replenished the high-lying fields. However, the fields in the Qingcheng City, Yangjiawei, Gaojiajian, and Furongwei areas in the northern countryside, which are the lowest-lying areas in the county, have been completely submerged, causing the farmers to show visible signs of worry.

Gaoyou 72

This was detected by people in the town, who reported it to the county government. A team was dispatched to arrest him. Trial of the Kidnapping and Abduction Case: Xiao Wangzi, the 17-year-old daughter of Chen Xiaobianzi, who runs a clothing store in Nanpingqiao in this city, was lured away in March of this year. Chen investigated everywhere and finally learned from Kong Xiaoruyizi that Chen Chen, a fellow business owner living in Daxiangkou, had enticed her. She was abducted and disappeared by a certain shop assistant of Mao Si, who runs a barbershop in Nanmen. She went to the county government to file a lawsuit. Yesterday (19th) at 6:00 PM, the plaintiffs, defendants, and witnesses, including Kong Xiaoruyizi, were summoned by Hu, the trial officer, to open a court for trial. As a result, Chen Chen was temporarily detained, Mao Si was released on bail, and a deadline was set to find the shop assistant and bring him to justice.

Maintenance Committee Borrows Money to Buy Rice: The price of rice in Shaoxing is soaring. The Grain Maintenance Committee is borrowing 13,000 bags of rice from Shanghai to sell at controlled prices in Shaoxing. In addition to the money for the first batch of 4,500 bags, which was allocated from the famine relief donation fund, the 8,500 bags of rice that arrived later were mortgaged to the bank, and 130,000 yuan in cash is urgently needed to redeem and open the rice for sale. Yesterday, the county government convened a joint meeting of the banking and currency industries at the County Chamber of Commerce on the 22nd to discuss ways to borrow money.

Total Number of Yangmei Exported in the Past Week: Yangmei is a specialty of this county, with varieties such as Crystal, Original Sand, and Rose. There are 500 to 600 families involved in this industry throughout the county, with exports worth 200,000 yuan. However, it is only a one-season industry every year in May and June, especially in Yangjiaxi, Xujia, Aozhaoao, and Baimahu in the Second District. The plum trees on the mountains in these areas have been particularly lush this year due to the continuous spring rains. According to an investigation of people in this industry, in the week from the 13th to the 19th, the total number of yangmei transported to Shanghai, Hangzhou, Ningbo, Yue, and other places was approximately 18,000 baskets.

Rice Prices Rise Again: Since the beginning of spring in this county, rice prices have gradually soared without any hope of falling. The poor and small vendors are greatly alarmed. According to people in the rice industry, there is a risk of continued price increases. Widow Dies from Illegal Abortion: A certain widow in Jinhai, Xixiang, Zhaura, worked as a helper in Shanghai due to family discord. Unexpectedly, the widow became pregnant with someone, and delivery was imminent. So she returned to Zha and went to Zhong Sanhe, an elderly midwife in her seventies on Ban Jing street, to seek an abortion. Zhong used an abortifacient. But the placenta failed to come out. Surgical operation then injured some of the internal parts, with excessive blood loss and she became more and more weak. She was sent to Chengji Hospital with hospital Director Yan Jiesheng for treatment, but she was already almost breathless. Director Yan reported it to the Public Security Bureau. After Chief Duanmu went to the hospital and clarified the situation, she refused to guarantee her life before surgery was performed. Later, the placenta was removed, and a cardiac stimulant was given, but it was ineffective. In just a few minutes, the woman passed away. Upon inspecting her body, a pair of gold earrings weighing about two qian and seventeen silver dollars were found. This was her ticket to sell coffins and to prepare for the funeral which will be temporarily kept in the wasteland outside the North Gate, awaiting recognition by her family.

Qiantang Tide is a Spectacular Sight: The period for viewing the tide on the Qiantang River is not far away. The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau annually opens special trains during the tide season to facilitate travel. However, the viewing locations in previous years, such as Zhijiang Qian in Hangzhou and Shangtang in Haining, were all within the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railway line, allowing passengers to travel at their convenience. This year, the Railway Bureau, considering the tide conditions, believes that Haining County is the best location and intends to designate Haining as the viewing location, which would boost the local economy. It has sent a letter to the Zhejiang Department of Civil Affairs for review. The department believed that it was impossible to determine whether it was appropriate to designate Haining as the viewing location, so it has submitted a report to the Provincial Government, requesting that the county conduct a review and provide a response to inform the decision.

Educational News

Important News: The Jiangsu Education Department Issues an Order for the 19th Year

Key Points for Social Education Facilities 82

Operational Expenses Should Account for Thirty Percent

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, in order to review and distribute the key points for social education facilities in various counties for the 19th year, orders the Education Bureaus of various counties to comply and implement them. The order states that, although efforts have been made to promote social education in various counties over the past three years, and a considerable foundation has been established, due to the fact that all facilities are mostly of a pioneering and experimental nature, they have not yet been fully perfected in practice. Now that the 19th year is about to begin, it is necessary to show the target and clearly indicate the path, so that the counties know where to turn for social education facilities, which is not enough to provide a model and facilitate promotion. The department, in view of this, has specially formulated twenty-two key points for social education facilities in various counties for the 19th year. In addition to distribution, a copy will be sent to the Bureau Directors, who are ordered to immediately comply and implement them. This is of utmost importance. This order.

Key Points for Attention Regarding Social Education Facilities 83

(1) The most important principle for social education facilities this year is to improve the lives of the people, promote local autonomy, and advance the work of political tutelage. (2) All facilities should focus on the widespread promotion of rural areas, and concentrate the majority of material and spiritual resources on adult literacy education. (3) All facilities should develop comprehensive plans for the entire county, create specific programs, and individual implementation procedures, and submit them to the Department of Education for approval before implementing them earnestly.

(4) Based on appropriate objective standards, divide the entire county into several public education districts, and designate public education centers or farmers' education centers as the central institutions for implementing urban and rural public education within the district. The aforementioned central institutions for implementing public education should coordinate with other administrative and educational institutions.

(5) The establishment of central institutions for implementing public education should be phased in, but within this year, at least two to four institutions should be established in the most needed areas, based on economic capacity and the number of districts. The organization should be as simple as possible, aiming to use fewer personnel and accomplish more. (6) To implement adult literacy education, the following committees should be organized, first following the provincial methods: (1) Literacy Movement Committee, (2) Phonetic Symbols Promotion Committee, (3) Public School Promotion Committee. When necessary, items (2) and (3) may be combined into item (1) for handling.

(7) Public schools, in addition to establishing specialized schools as much as possible, all agencies and schools should uniformly establish them as annexes. Detailed regulations for the annexes will be issued separately.

(8) Public schools should hold two terms each year, and complete graduation within the prescribed time limit for each term. Teaching hours do not necessarily have to be at night, and should be based on the convenience of the learners.

(9) In places where public schools cannot be established, or where class-based teaching is not applicable, literacy centers and inquiry centers should be widely established, and mobile teaching methods should be adopted as a substitute.

(10) In places where literacy education is developed, or where there is group living, higher-level public schools and vocational supplementary schools for farmers, workers, and businesses should be piloted. Their organizational structure should be flexible, and they should all equally emphasize civic training. (11) Libraries and gymnasiums should be established uniformly in counties where they have not yet been established. In counties where they have already been established, they should be promoted appropriately, with the goal of balanced development with the central institutions implementing public education.

(12) Various social education institutions other than libraries and gymnasiums should be promoted appropriately according to the actual needs and economic conditions of each county.

(13) All existing social education institutions should uniformly streamline their organizations, and find ways to enrich their content and increase efficiency. Their industrial expenditures should account for at least 30% of the total funding of the institution.

(14) Regarding the improvement of customs and the promotion of public entertainment, appropriate methods should be carefully formulated based on local conditions and actively implemented.

(16) Various public education movements, such as the literacy movement and the hygiene movement, should be earnestly held.

(17) The responsible personnel of all agencies and enterprises should give priority to hiring personnel who have received specialized training in social education.

(18) The performance of all agencies should be strictly evaluated, and the bureau should establish social education supervisors to supervise and urge.

(19) The original and newly added social education funds should be absolutely guaranteed to be independent and should not be diverted to other undertakings outside of social education. If this provision is violated, the funds diverted should be compensated by the director of the bureau privately, and the department will give appropriate administrative sanctions.

(20) Social education funds that have been approved in the budget, and the funds that social education should receive from the reserve funds, may be approved for use due to the definite needs of social education undertakings.

(21) If a farmers' education center has indeed achieved considerable success in expanding its operations, it may be approved to use civil affairs and educational funds specifically designated for this purpose, in addition to the tax on paper.

(22) Accumulated social education funds from before the 18th year, and various social education expenditures for the 19th year, shall not be used without approval. In addition, social education funds that were diverted before the 18th year, after being investigated and recovered, should be used exclusively to compensate for the accumulated deficits in social education funds. If there is a surplus, it should be stored as a social education accumulation fund, and all should be submitted for approval before being disbursed and stored separately.

Order from the Ministry

Summer School Credit Not Counted 84

The Ministry of Education instructs the Departments of Education of all provinces and municipalities to avoid instructing all schools above the secondary level to run summer schools, originally for the purpose of supplementary studies and advanced study for faculty and staff, and not to immediately calculate summer school grades as credits.

Ministry Order: Yanjing University to Abolish Religious Department 85

The Ministry of Education believes that the advertisement for new students at Peking Yanjing University includes a specialized department for religious undertakings and social service, which clearly has a propaganda role for religion. It will immediately instruct the Peking Municipal Bureau of Education to order the school to abolish the subject immediately, and the Bureau will check from time to time whether the subject has stopped proceeding.

Xiamen Jimei School Aiding Ye's Trend 86

Principal and Director Resign

Students Strike and Petition

Jimei School Because the summer vacation has arrived, and School Director Ye Cai Zhen was detained by the Siming District Court in the Xu case, and has repeatedly requested bail, but has not achieved the purpose, faculty, staff and students are very accustomed and excited. One is that the budget meeting has not been held, and the progress plan for the next semester has not been approved. In fact, there is a trend that it cannot start school. The other is that the central government is headless, and there is an uneasy phenomenon in the school. Teachers have no intention, and scholars are boring. Therefore, the overall resignation and strike occurred. The court does not allow bail and does not quickly investigate and pronounce judgment. Human rights are obstructed. What is the benefit of running a school? Please allow me to resign. Jimei Middle School, Fisheries and Commerce, Agriculture and Forestry, Girls' Middle School, Kindergarten Teacher, Male and Female Elementary School Principals, Secretariat General Affairs Office, Accounting Office, Science Museum, Library, Hospital, and Education Promotion Department. Yuan, I heard that after this telegram was sent, the situation was also notified to the overseas Chinese in various ports of Nanyang and newspapers and communities across the country. If the school stops running, the responsibility for the loss of more than 2,000 students in the middle of the road is very important, and southern Fujian education will also go bankrupt from now on.

On the student side, due to their own interests, they convened a general meeting on May 12 and proposed to organize a human rights protection association. Some said that the name of this association was inappropriate and had been banned in various places and could not be used. Others proposed to organize a freedom liberation association, but because the scope was too broad, it was not passed. Later, it was decided to organize a joint federation of student self-government associations of various schools. The representative of fisheries wanted to add the words "temporary", while the representative of the middle school wanted to set it as a permanent organization. There was a lot of discussion and each insisted on his own opinion. Fearing that it would delay the opportunity, the middle school continued to meet separately on the 13th and resolved to strike. At dawn on the 14th, each group elected five representatives to take a motorboat to Xiamen to petition. A total of 65 representatives, led by the sports director Zhuang, arrived at the Siming Court, with tight security, as if facing a formidable enemy. The representatives went straight up to the small building without any joy, and were personally received by the president Deng Ji'an. After talking for a long time, President Deng said that the case was handled by prosecutor Ouyang Han. Ouyang Han was away on official business and would convey the feelings to the representatives when he returned. The representatives strongly requested the release of School Director Ye on bail. President Deng said that according to legal procedures, the prosecutor should make the final decision. The final appointment was made for further discussion, and dispersed." The representatives returned to the school, and the results were incomplete. The methods of dredging are other schools. Seeing the enthusiasm of the middle school, they are also eager to try the kindergarten normal school students with only a hundred people. They will continue to petition on the day of their return. It is said that the school is designing a large-scale petition, knowing that it is difficult for all 2,000 people to go to Xiamen at the same time, they will go by boat and car in stages in advance. After all of them arrive, they will gather in Gulangyu, Xiamen to march and petition until they achieve their goal.

The students of the school have been busy traveling back and forth for several days, and the cost of boats and cars is considerable. The method of raising money is also very new. According to the school's regulations, breakfast is porridge, and lunch and dinner are rice. Since May 13, the student self-government association has announced that all meals will be porridge, and the surplus meal expenses will be used to pay for petition travel expenses.

Recent News from the Jiangsu Provincial Agricultural Education Center 88

Investigation and Improvement of Wheat Harvest Results

Editing the Overview of the Provincial Agricultural Education Center

The Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Education Center sold twelve stones, nine dou, seven liters, and five he of improved wheat seeds last year to 69 households, and guided the planting methods by household. Now that the harvest season has arrived, the center has investigated the harvest results and found that the number of acres planted is 259 acres and 5 fen, the total harvest is 196 stones, two dou, nine liters, and nine he, the average yield per acre is seven dou and five liters and six he, the best yield per acre is one stone and three dou, and the minimum yield per acre is six dou. The average harvest per acre is two dou more than the local variety, it is said. The center recently adopted the principle of publishing cooperation and sent a circular to solicit the overview of the agricultural education centers in various counties, and compiled and printed it to promote it. The main points in the circular said that the cost will be shared based on the number of books taken. This method has several advantages: (1) If each center publishes and exchanges them separately, the printing cost will be more expensive due to the small number of copies, and more postage will be used. (2) If they are compiled into one book, the centers in other provinces and counties can send them to various provinces locally, and the provincial centers can send them separately. Each center only needs to order dozens of copies and donate them for reading in the territory. The publicity effect has reached the whole country. (3) Compilation is simpler and more comprehensive than separate publications, and it is easier to attract attention and be valued. (4) The center can compile statistics from the overview of each center and attach them to the book for research, and also plans 14 simple rules, stipulating that the collection period is until June 25, and the book will be published at the end of July. Those who order 25 copies will pay six yuan, those who order 50 copies will pay ten yuan, those who order 75 copies will pay fourteen yuan, and those who order 100 copies will pay eighteen yuan. The provincial agricultural education center and the agricultural education centers in various counties will share the book fees. The surplus will be returned, and the shortage will be supplemented by the provincial agricultural education center. After receiving the circular, the centers responded and submitted manuscripts, which was quite enthusiastic, it is said.

Summary of Summer Educational Administration in Guangdong Education Department (1) Yi Lu 91

Formulating work plans for junior high school and specialized fields

Submitted to the Ministry of Education for inspection, verification, and record for implementation

The Guangdong Province Summer Junior High School and Educational Administration have been carefully planned by the Department of Education, including elementary education, secondary education, and higher education. According to the situation and the urgency of the matters to be handled, the outline will be implemented. There are nine items in the outline and dozens of detailed items. The implementation period is from April to June. The following is the detailed work plan for the three months: First, (Elementary Education) (A) Preparation for the implementation of compulsory education. Checking and parallel education are recorded in the party program. However, the popularization of education is based on the promotion of compulsory education. During this period of political tutelage, it is even more important to organize it. We have received Instruction No. 529 from the University Council, ordering us to vigorously implement compulsory education, etc. The Guangdong Provincial Compulsory Education Committee has been organized, and the counties and cities have been ordered to follow it. Due to military influence, the Provincial Compulsory Education Committee has not yet been established, and only a few Compulsory Education Committees have been established in the counties and cities. Now that the overall situation is gradually stable, the Provincial Compulsory Education Committee plans to be established soon, and at the same time, it urges the counties and cities to organize soon. During this period, a thorough investigation of school-age children will be conducted, and the counties will be ordered to establish at least one rural normal school in each county before August of the 19th year in order to store teachers and facilitate progress, so that the plan to reduce the number of out-of-school children year by year can be realized. (B) Urge the counties and cities to increase the number of elementary schools in stages to reduce the number of out-of-school children. The plan has been promulgated by the Ministry of Education and has been distributed for compliance. The elementary schools in the counties and cities of the province are not enough to accommodate out-of-school children according to the survey statistics. It is planned to issue another order urging the counties and cities to make a comprehensive plan, raise funds widely, increase the number of elementary schools in districts, and ban private schools, advocate or subsidize private elementary schools, and draw up a complete plan before the beginning of the 19th year and submit it to the department for approval and implementation. (C) Urge private elementary schools to register. The regulations on the registration of private schools have been promulgated for a long time, and the elementary schools in each prefecture must all register anew, and have been followed in accordance with the Ministry's orders. Now, the elementary schools in each county and city have previously applied for registration, but have not reorganized and reported in accordance with the regulations, and have reported to the counties and cities for approval and established them rashly. It is planned to issue an order separately to report and register as soon as possible in order to follow the unified standard and comply with the regulations. (D) Register various normal school graduates. To promote elementary schools, it is necessary to cultivate teachers first. According to the survey, most of the elementary school teachers in each prefecture are not normal school graduates. In the future, the lack of teachers in the newly established elementary schools will be even more serious. The current remedial measures are to first register various normal school graduates and distribute them to the counties and cities as soon as possible for employment. Moreover, after registration and statistics, the number of existing normal school graduates in various places can be known, and there will be a basis for planning the training of teachers in the future. It is planned that the department will formulate measures and issue an order to the counties and cities to extend the registration period. (E) Formulate measures for summer training courses for elementary school teachers in various counties and cities. Educational trends are constantly changing, and teaching methods are constantly improving. Then, the teachers' cultivation is still there. However, most of the elementary school teachers are class teachers, and there is very little time left outside of the homework. It is planned to use the summer vacation to hold meetings and lectures, so that elementary school teachers can cultivate themselves in time and directly improve the teachers' knowledge, that is, indirectly improve the teaching of elementary schools. The detailed measures for the lectures will be formulated by the department and uniformly implemented by the counties and cities before the summer vacation of the 19th year. (F) Formulate measures for summer vacation schools in elementary schools. Summer vacation schools in elementary schools mean that elementary school students still have to go to school for a certain amount of time every day during the summer vacation to make up for their studies, or be guided by faculty and staff to work, or for various games and sports, or for study tours. Some counties and cities have already run this kind of summer vacation school, and there are some achievements. It is planned that the department will formulate measures and uniformly hold them in the counties and cities during the summer vacation of the 19th year, and the implementation will be called for by the department for assessment.

The Call for the Promotion of Overseas Chinese Education Association 92

The Overseas Chinese Education Design Committee Will Hold a Plenary Committee

Liu Shimu and Li Denghui Propose the Formulation of Regulations for the Overseas Chinese Education Association. The Ministry of Education, in order to improve and promote Overseas Chinese education, has specially established the Overseas Chinese Education Design Committee, which has already announced its establishment. It is scheduled to hold its second plenary committee meeting in Beijing on June 25th to discuss various important issues. Committee members Liu Shimu and Li Denghui have submitted a proposal to formulate regulations for the Overseas Chinese Education Association. The original text is now transcribed below:

Since the Central Party Headquarters and Jinan University successively convened Overseas Chinese education conferences to resolve various Overseas Chinese education issues, and then the Second National Education Conference also passed a comprehensive plan to improve Overseas Chinese education, the plan for Overseas Chinese affairs can be said to be well-prepared. However, the resolutions are valuable in their implementation, and the method of implementation must be defined by regulations and detailed rules for compliance. This is a necessary procedure in administration. According to the resolutions on Overseas Chinese education at the Second National Education Conference, the most important and detailed measure is to establish the Overseas Chinese Education Association as the first step. This proposal was previously discussed at the Overseas Chinese education conference convened by the Central Training Department and a decision was made to formulate organizational regulations to be promulgated by the Ministry of Education. However, it has not yet been promulgated, and it is not known which agency is drafting these regulations or where they are being reviewed and approved. This committee is responsible for design, and cannot ignore this matter. A draft should first be prepared and submitted to the Central Party Headquarters for review, and then submitted to the Ministry of Education for promulgation. Now, several principles for the regulations of the Overseas Chinese Education Association are proposed, and the election of drafters is requested to be done immediately. Is this appropriate? We await public decision.

Principles for Formulating Regulations for the Overseas Chinese Education Association

1. The purpose of this Association is to research and develop Overseas Chinese education and assist in Overseas Chinese education administration. 2. Members of this Association include all current and former Overseas Chinese school teachers and staff, and those who are enthusiastic about Overseas Chinese affairs and have contributed to Overseas Chinese education. 3. This Association adopts a committee system. The General Association has nine to eleven committee members, with five or three standing members. Overseas branches have five to seven committee members, with three or one standing member. Committee members are elected by the general membership meeting. However, in the initial stage of the establishment of branches, the General Association may send personnel to prepare. 4. The headquarters of the General Association is located in the capital. The location of overseas branches shall be decided by the General Association Committee through overall planning. It is also possible to establish branches in important ports first. 5. Membership fees are two yuan per person per year. Other expenses are covered by the Ministry of Education from the Overseas Chinese education fund. Branches may receive subsidies from the General Association or raise funds locally. 6. After the establishment of this Association, all existing overseas education associations must reorganize into branches. If there are differences in powers and organizations, they must be reviewed and approved by the General Association.

The Content of the Wusong Merchant Marine School 99

Today, our country's shipping materials are extremely depleted. It is not only the merchant ships that are like this, but also the navy is in short supply, and there is a sigh of difficulty in finding talent. The Wusong Merchant Marine School of the Ministry of Communications, since its restoration last year, is the only place in our country that cultivates shipping materials. Recently, someone went to visit and had a two-hour conversation with the school's executives. I recorded what they said and summarized it into five items: history, doctrine, equipment, grades, and treatment. It is also what those who care about shipping affairs are happy to hear.

History The school was initiated by Zhang Ji, Tang Weizhi, Sheng Xingcun and other gentlemen during the Xuantong period. They requested the Qing court to allocate 60 mu of the military camp site in Paotai Bay, Wusong, to build school buildings, break away from the naval administration department of Nanyang University, and become an independent school directly under the Ministry of Communications in Beijing. General Sa Dingming, a veteran of the navy, was hired as the principal. The comprehensiveness of the equipment and the excellence of the faculty were unparalleled in the school for a time. In the third year of Xuantong, the first enrollment was held at Nanyang University, and more than 3,000 people registered. The selection was meticulous, and they were all cautious and studious. Later, the students served on merchant ships, breaking the foreign monopoly on the shipping profession, and pioneering the Chinese to serve as captains. To this day, most of the Chinese ship captains and those who preside over important positions in the shipping industry are still former students. Unfortunately, it was closed down in the fourth year of the Republic due to some reason. The school buildings were changed by the Navy Department to run a naval officer school, which resulted in no one rising up later, creating the phenomenon that there is an insufficient supply of crew members in the country today. Otherwise, foreign crew members would have disappeared from Chinese ships long ago. How could this have been expected? When the National Government was established, Minister of Communications Wang Boqun, in view of the fact that the shipping industry was a top priority and that the cultivation of shipping materials could not be delayed, resolutely proposed it. After the Central Political Conference approved the re-establishment of the school, it reopened in the autumn of the 18th year. Minister Wang was publicly elected as the principal, and Yang Zhixiong, a former classmate, was appointed as the deputy. Yang Jun made great efforts to prepare for the restoration of the school. During the 14 years of closure, time and circumstances changed and everything was destroyed. All the instruments, books, machines, school equipment, medicines, and all kinds of sundries worth more than 100,000 yuan disappeared. Now, we are trying to restore the old appearance from the ashes of the robbery. Even the slightest of grass and trees has to be done by hand. The management will be the same as planting trees and nurturing people. Those who lightly destroy the world, how can they know the difficulty of construction? It is regrettable.

Doctrine The school's teaching doctrine is not only to enable students to understand the theory in the textbooks, but also to emphasize the familiarity with practical work. Nowadays, those who practice driving often do not understand the outline of the use of sails and the skills of sailors, and those who practice the engine are craftsmen and apprentices. Those who have a little understanding of the principles of machinery management and construction are even rarer. Therefore, to remedy the shortcomings and correct the students' habit of looking down on themselves and disdaining to engage in labor, the usual education, such as factory practice, boat handling, and rope tying, can be painting, scrubbing, and physical exercise, all of which are equally important to the classroom work. Finally, they will take classes for two years in the school's self-built training ship to cultivate all-round talents before graduating.

Equipment The school's past equipment is as described above. Now, let me describe its current equipment. The equipment that has been purchased includes a basic compass, a small boat compass, a bearing mirror, a depth sounder, a meridian instrument, a sextant, a rangefinder, a positioning instrument, a self-counting barometer, a silver barometer, a depth gauge, a steering wheel, a nautical chart, a wireless radio, and a generator key. There are also a rotating compass, a wireless radio positioning instrument, and an echo depth sounder, all of which are installed in the practice board. The library focuses on nautical books, and there are already more than 1,000 books. There are also thousands of books that have been ordered from various countries in the East and West but have not yet arrived. There are two sampans, each of which can accommodate 20 people, and 50 life jackets are provided. Practice rowing in the Wusong River estuary at a specified time. There are two large and small drill grounds with an area of more than 230,000 square feet. Basketball, football, tennis, billiards, table tennis, and running tracks are all complete. There is one indoor and one outdoor swimming pool. The indoor pool uses邦浦打水, and the outdoor pool is 360 feet long and 75 feet wide. The volume is large. It takes time to use邦浦, so a 500-foot iron pipe will be installed in the pool to connect to the river and use the tide to change the water in the pool. However, it is necessary to obtain the consent of the Public Works Bureau and the 濬浦 Bureau after passing through the road outside the school and the land along the shore before the reconstruction can be carried out. It is already in progress. The machine factory will start construction during the summer vacation this year and will be completed in four months. It will be equipped with a 100-horsepower boiler, generator, machine tool, sand turning field, and other mechanical parts. In addition, a school ship will be built for students to practice on from 1931. It is estimated to be 300 feet long, with a speed of 14 knots, a full-load draft of 16 feet 6 inches, a double-bottom steel plate, a load of 3,000 tons, and will sail to the northern and southern ports of China and various places in Japan and Nanyang. The estimated cost is 1 million yuan. As soon as the government approves it, bids will be invited for construction.

Grades The school has three departments: driving, engine, and crew training courses. In 1929, two driving classes were recruited first. In 1930, one driving class and two engine classes were recruited. After that, one driving and one engine class will be recruited every year. By 1933, the first graduates of the driving department will be assigned to various ships to serve as crew members. Step by step, it will not take ten years to clear out foreign crew members and replace them with Chinese.

Treatment The school treats students with the best possible conditions. The crew profession is inherently difficult. If they are not accustomed to hard work and content with simple living, even if they graduate, they will not be able to devote themselves to it. And the sons of wealthy families are usually fond of leisure. How can they be willing to work hard in this noble profession? Those who are happy to do this and come to study must be outstanding, unique, or have aspirations to learn, and are heartbroken that the shipping industry is controlled by others, strive to be strong, and hope to restore it in the future. These are all outstanding people of the time. The school upholds the purpose of cultivating talents, so it treats students well and tries its best to reduce their burden. It only charges 50 yuan for food expenses for the whole year. Uniforms and books are self-provided, and all other expenses are not charged. It is also working hard to plan for their future after graduation. The Ministry will issue crew certificates, and they can be employed as crew members.
