Free Talk

Words of One Gained, Qiu Shui 104

Before marriage, women close their eyes to be kissed by men. After marriage, when their men forget to kiss them, they close their eyes.

Life reaches fifty-five, all things are over, and it is an era when one can realize oneself. After the age of fifty-five, if a man wants to win the favor of young women, he can only play the role of Santa Claus, and there is no possibility of being "Tang Rouan" (a beautiful man of ancient times).

Death is a great adventure, but "marriage" is the greatest adventure, because marriage is a path to a new life, a beginning of a new life, a strange thing of living with someone who is completely unknown.

"Success" kills people more fiercely than artillery fire, and love kills people even more than "success."

A person with a clear mind often encounters accidents that are not taken seriously by fools.

When a woman's address is no longer remembered by any men, and her old nickname is often mentioned by them, this woman has no happiness to speak of, and her nickname is as unremarkable as a phone number.

Modern women have a calm attitude and precise plans. How do I know this? Because before marriage, they often return all the engagement rings they have received to their original owners without error.

Love is blind, but "marriage" is a good medicine for curing blindness. Therefore, the best way for men and women to know each other's hearts is to get married.

Record of the Tragic Robbery in Shizhuang, Zhong Huan 105

Rugao is remotely located on the north bank of the Yangtze River in Jiangsu. Since the spring of the 16th year of the Republic of China, Sun Jun relied on the Yangtze River as a trapped beast to fight. The city of Rugao was ravaged by it, but the six districts of Shizhuang, Lugang, Zhuntao, Chema Lake, Motou, and Jiang'an in the southwest along the river suffered even more. After the national army defeated them, many of them wandered to the local area. They were idle and had no way to make a living, so they formed gangs and robbed people on the road. Then, they kidnapped people for ransom, harassing them for three or four years. Although the military police have been suppressing and arresting them, they have not been able to eliminate them. Those who used to rely on farming for a living did not dare to cultivate, industry and commerce were suspended, the market was depressed, and the food supply was almost cut off. As a result, the slightly wealthy fled to the city walls and other ports. The violent people took risks and joined the bandits. Among these six districts, Shizhuang Town is the most important (commonly known as Shizhuang Lane). It is about 2 miles away from the river bank. The Tongyang wheel sails back and forth, and docks on the bank to load and unload goods. Since the rampant of bandits, the town has increased the number of military police to protect merchants and residents, and also goes to the suburbs to arrest bandits from time to time. Those who are serious offenders are immediately beheaded and displayed to the public. Those who are minor offenders are released on bail. The military police in the town went to a certain place a few days ago and arrested four bandits. Two of them were indeed wanted criminals. They were immediately beheaded and hung on the stone bridge. The other two were detained in prison for interrogation. The bandits heard the news and gathered more than a thousand people at about 4 pm on the 11th to attack from the northwest. There were six military police stationed at the north end of the town. They could not defend themselves and were rushed into the streets. They set fire to the houses. The town's security corps, the Public Security Bureau, and the 3rd squadron of the county police stationed there heard the news and immediately went to resist. Gunshots rang out, one after another. After holding on for a long time, the military police were about to run out of ammunition. Some advocated retreating. Captain Tang (Che Ru) of the garrison unit told the soldiers, "The units stationed in the east and west ports heard the news

Mould Season Musings · Soup · Brush Flower 106

It's the season of mould. The weather is erratic. We must know a thing or two about common sense regarding the mould season. Here, I will gather what I have seen and set it down as follows.

The mould season is the time when all things are damp and steaming. The human body is no exception. Therefore, one must bathe once every day so that the sweat pores are open and unobstructed, and excretion is easy. Avoid eating various pickled foods, such as mouldy fermented bean curd, soy paste, pickled cucumbers, and stinky dried tofu.

Clothes must be changed frequently, quilts and blankets must be aired frequently, windows must be opened frequently, and floors must be washed frequently.

Pour plenty of disinfectant water into the ditches to avoid foul odours. Regularly burn incense coils indoors to add fragrance. It is especially good to plant flowering plants in the courtyard.

Do not fold clothes that have been soaked by continuous rain. They must be hung in a ventilated place.

Alcohol can aggravate dampness, especially during the mould season. You must abstain from drinking it.

If you can follow the above methods, you can avoid illness and maintain good health.

Must come to the rescue. We defend but do not attack. Bullets must not be fired wildly. (Dongxin Rising Port is two li west, Zhang Huang Port is eight li away, the Third Detachment is stationed at these two ports.) Otherwise, all the houses in the town will be reduced to scorched earth. Before long, the detachments from both ports came to assist. Captain Tang then commanded the military police to attack fiercely. After five hours, the bandits could not hold out and retreated. It was already late at night. The next day at dawn, six more bandits sneaked into the central market of the town, setting fires with straw. They were discovered by the military police. One was shot and killed, and the rest escaped. Many large and small households were looted in this battle, making it impossible to investigate. More than one hundred houses were destroyed. Captain Tang of the Central Detachment was wounded in the arm, and four police officers suffered minor injuries. Xu Wan Cheng, the owner of the Xu Fu Sheng Sugar Shop, was wounded in both his arm and legs. The dead were Liu Huan, the captain of the Seventh Detachment, and police officer Huang Ke Wen. About ten other residents were killed by stray bullets. Also, a certain family was preparing for a funeral after someone had died of illness not long before, but the body was also burned to charcoal in the arson. It was truly tragic. It is now said that the local authorities in Ru Yi are planning to organize a disaster relief committee for the six southwestern districts. However, the bandits have not been cleared, agriculture is abandoned in the fields, and industry and commerce have ceased. Even if relief grain is distributed, it will be a drop in the bucket. What good will it do? (Qu Que)

Travel Miscellany - Oh, the Habit 107

A Trip to Chuzhou. Chuzhou is one of the major stations on the southern section of the Jinpu Railway. The distance from Pukou to here is 105 li. The total length of the Jinpu Line is 1,900 li. From Pukou to Xuzhou is the southern section, from Xuzhou to Jinan is the central section, and from Jinan to Tianjin is the northern section, each being six or seven hundred li long. In the past, it only took 21 hours to complete the entire line. Now, each section takes 21 hours. The fare is also almost doubled. This is because, in addition to a price increase of about 30%, there is also a "repair fee" that passengers must bear. However, the deterioration of road administration, the dilapidation of vehicles, and the discomfort of passengers are in direct opposition to the continuous increase in fares. Currently, during the military period, seven or eight out of ten passengers ride without tickets. Railway workers can only shake their heads and sigh.

Chuzhou is famous for Ouyang Xiu's "Record of the Pavilion of the Old Drunkard." Almost all scholars know the phrase "Mountains surround Chuzhou." And "The Old Drunkard's intention is not in the wine" is an even more common allusion. However, an examination of the actual situation reveals that this is not the case. The Chuzhou area is not surrounded by many mountains. There are only small hills in the south of the city, and the north is mostly plains. Small hills, under Ouyang Xiu's pen, become large mountain peaks that encircle and overlap. The difference in perspective is like this.

The Pavilion of the Old Drunkard has long been dilapidated. The rebuilt version is located ten li from the station at the foot of Mount Langya. It has some scenery. Below is the Langya Stream, also known as Brewing Spring. The geography of ancient and modern times has not changed much. To the west of Chuzhou is Qingliu Pass, where Emperor Taizu of the Song Dynasty defeated Li Jing's army of 100,000 soldiers and captured his generals Yao Feng and Huangfu Hui. In addition, there are scenic spots such as Fengle Pavilion and Tea Immortal Pavilion. Their names are certainly beautiful and elegant, but once you get there, you only see weeds, desolate smoke, dilapidated walls, and broken wells. Famous scenic spots are mostly like this.

Chuzhou relies on old-fashioned iron-wheeled rickshaws for transportation. These are all things that have been eliminated in the cities and have survived in the countryside. The wheels are made of wood instead of iron. Coupled with the dilapidated condition of the car body and the accumulation of roads

Nanyang Travelogue (33) Linghua 108

30th. Today I printed a name card. It cost one and a half yuan. It would cost no more than forty cents at home. One and a half yuan, when exchanged for national currency, is worth two and a half yuan. You can know the difference in living expenses here from home from this one aspect. Small workers earn one or two yuan a day. A rickshaw ride costs eight or nine cents an hour. Only haircuts are very cheap. It used to cost forty cents, but now it has been reduced to twenty cents. Small shops charge a dime and a half. Only the people here are more mature than those at home. There are fewer incidents of rampant bandits. The government provides good protection, and you can live and work in peace. The gates of the large mansions of the capitalists are still open, and they are not very worried about thieves. It is not like Shanghai, where people knock on doors and rob in broad daylight. This is not something you see here.

The Communist Party problem also exists occasionally. Slogans are occasionally found on the streets. But I heard that the method of prevention here is also different from that of our country. I heard that the Dutch method of prevention is the best. There is no pain at all. If someone is found to be advocating communism, they are not punished. They are only asked to realize their ideology in a certain place. This place is a desolate island in the middle of the sea. There are no ships coming and going. It is a place for exiled communists. There is land to cultivate. They are ordered to operate there forever. I heard that there are also women, but probably very few. This method is better than killing in our country. It seems that it is okay to imitate it.

The tram rules here are still good. Most of the drivers are Malays, and there are also Chinese. People are generally well-behaved. Their hospitality seems to be like the Japanese style. The trams in Beijing and Tianjin are also good. Only Shanghai is the worst, even below the Malays. Alas.

On the 31st, I visited an Indian church. It is roughly Brahmin. Various flowers are placed in the middle. I respectfully took off my shoes and entered. From the hall, I looked at the god they worshiped. In the pitch-black lamp, its face was black. It was suspicious and frightening, almost like the City God. India is a nation of polytheistic fantasies. There are many Indian-style Buddha statues and famous ones here. All show their fantasies. Most are like the Thousand-Handed Guanyin. They mostly regard the elephant as king. I know in Annam that they regard the tiger as king. They worship the tiger everywhere. India worships the elephant. Watching Indian paintings can cause people to hallucinate. It is also a way to unleash thoughts. I bought the most famous Indian painting to take home for my children to play with. The Buddha statues painted in various places in Japan are all like Japanese people. Northern paintings are like northern people. Western paintings are like western people. Indian paintings of Buddha statues are like Indian people. The Indian style of Buddha statues is the true Buddha statue. The Malays in the Nanyang region, although they worship Islam, are dominated by Indianization. Many monks here travel to India. I heard that it only costs one hundred yuan to go back and forth. Why don't the Buddhists in our country travel to India? Japanese people travel to India one after another. The local Indians, however, engage in petty trading. Those from Ji Ling sell. There are few big merchants. Recently, the Indian leader Gandhi was arrested. The Indians are gradually becoming more assertive. I heard that Tagore is not in India but in the UK. Tagore is a peaceful person, unlike Gandhi, who is a resistance faction.

In short, the trend in various parts of Nanyang is that the Philippines is independent, Siam is strong, and Burma and Annam are all starting revolutions. India is also the same. The future trend will inevitably lead to the establishment of a Nanyang federation. It is only a matter of time.

The dirt matched. I heard that in previous years, during bountiful harvests, the market was quite lively. Now, however, years of drought have made farmers appear emaciated. The market has greatly declined. This is no doubt related to the military situation.

Chuzhou has the Ninth Normal School of Anhui Province. The school is located in the west of the city. It has a lot of scenery. The campus is full of lush trees and shallow grass. It is a pity that the sounds of reading have stopped for a long time, and the students are scattered. Now, only a few fragments of Western-style buildings remain.

I once visited a small primary school in Chuzhou City. I only saw that the students were all handsome and lovely. Unfortunately, it has now been converted into a hospital for wounded soldiers. Alas.

European Correspondence (60) Liu Haipiao 109

French Autumn Salon 丨 1929 SalondAutomne1929

(2) A brief history of the Autumn Salon

Only a few years later, the Autumn Salon had already swept through most of the Europeans of the time. There were even many people who regarded the producers of the Autumn Salon as idols. Being able to produce the Autumn Salon was a great honour. This was the pure aspiration of European artists. Especially many of the big shots opened up public roads for new trends from different aspects. Without narrowly or superficially establishing factions to limit production. As long as you have good things and fresh creations, you can be included in the list. It is not based on paintings by Bonnard or Matisse as the standard. Nor is it dominated by Van Dangen or Marguai. Nor does it mean that Trang Derain Guerlain or anyone else is considered a follower. It is a simultaneous combination of all writers who are incompatible but have new life to oppose that dead, boring, and decadent art, that is, to rebel against the traditional art of the government.

From this point of view, it is a transformation in art. Looking at the whole thing, it is a transformation in thought. Modern people's lives are always moving towards the "dynamic" and "active" aspects. Although we don't understand it ourselves, we are always moving towards new aspects. This is indeed the case. We are living. We are always moving towards the fresh hope of the future. We hope for a glorious era in the future. So we desperately want to move towards the "living" side. Those who silently abide by tradition, are content with a static, dead life, and believe in maintaining the status quo are already lagging behind the times. They are merely possessing a body without a spirit. They are equivalent to the already dead. Therefore, modern, true, and profound art must move towards the "dynamic" and "active." It establishes a kind of life from the creative aspect. However, in China, where art knowledge is extremely naive, a generation of vulgar people, how can they understand the beauty of colour, the beauty of form, the internal life and profound rhythm of art? They take drawing the head and painting the corners as beautiful. They consider painting history, legends, or patriotic paintings to be noble subjects. They only know the superficial outer form. They do not understand the true meaning of art at all. Even ordinary people who claim to be painters are full of such vulgar views. They regard describing the dead outer form and worshiping the end skills of the official school as something to be proud of. These people can paint a few portraits for the rich and earn some money, but they cannot really talk about modern valuable art, because he is already a dead person with only a body and no soul. This situation is also unavoidable in France. There are also many vulgar artisans like this. But they have already been abandoned to the lower classes and excluded from the modern art scene.

I have already digressed slightly from the topic. Now let's get back to the point. The Autumn Salon has already become the general organization of the modern art scene. But there are still those vulgar people who hold opposing attitudes.

The reason why the Autumn Salon can have such authority is thanks to a dictator. He used the strict organization of the French Republic to organize the sacred Autumn Salon. This dictator is the madman Frantz Jourdain

The strangest thing is that the two most prominent and authoritative salons are both under the rule of a dictator. No one in Europe doesn't know that Shardan combined the spirit of Lenin and Mussolini into one to engage in the artistic revolution movement and be the protector of new art. Shardan is the chairman of the Autumn Salon, just like Paul Signae is the chairman of the Independent Exhibition SsocietedeArtistesIndependato. Although their personalities are different, sometimes even extremely opposite. But each one tries his best to protect the authority of a salon is equally great.

The history of the Autumn Salon can be said to be intertwined with the history of its dictator. The Autumn Salon's current and future development is mostly due to his capacity.

New York's Silk Sales Are Weak After the Implementation of the New Tariff Act

The Summer Silkworm Crop in the Mainland Is Not Good, and the Cost of Silk for Chinese Merchants Is Difficult to Relax

The transaction of Chinese silk last week almost came to a standstill. In previous years, after the new silk came on the market, European and American merchants would throw and purchase forward silk for each month, and the market would have a smooth period. This year, it is dying, and there is a tendency to be unable to recover. Since the surge in the gold market, the exchange rate of the shilling has changed repeatedly. The sales of British and French silk fabrics are sluggish. Silk factories have to use artificial silk to reduce costs due to concerns about the unemployment of workers. As a result, artificial silk floods the market and competes for sales. Last week, there were only sporadic spot transactions of Chinese and Japanese raw silk. Since the implementation of the new tariff act in New York, the stock market has plummeted, and a major panic has occurred in the economic world. Raw silk factories cannot sell, and silk prices fall frequently. Overseas silk cables are not transferred. Chinese silk merchants believe that the summer silkworm crop in the mainland has suffered damage due to the weather. The Zhejiang cocoons are in short supply, and the price of cocoons is increasingly high. Silkworm diseases are rampant in Jiangsu Province, and a bumper harvest is unlikely. In the future, the raw materials will be scarce, and the cost of silk will still be difficult to lower. Selling at a loss is impossible due to the situation, and European and American merchants are also watching from the sidelines. This is the general reason for the stagnation of silk sales last week. Last week, more than one hundred bales of spot silk were traded, and more than one thousand bales of old silk were sold. Western firms cleared their old silk, and 400 pieces of new silk were shipped to France. Overseas Chinese silk is uniformly sold at a low price.

Southern and Northern Goods and Sichuan Pickled Mustard Tuber Arrivals Are Blocked, and the Trend Is Brisk 119

Recently, the source of Sichuan pickled mustard tuber has been cut off due to traffic obstructions there. The goods stored here have been opened to 31 or 32 yuan by merchants. However, now they want to increase the price under the pretext of the temporary interruption of the source. The trend is particularly tight. As for sales destinations such as Guangdong and Shantou, digestion is quite smooth. Secondly, inland markets are also continuous. The firms sell at 28 or 29 yuan, and the secondary firms sell at 25 or 26 yuan. Good-quality goods from special firms are also sold for more than 30 yuan. The market situation will also tend to rise afterward, as the merchants' market is tight.

The Sugar Market Is Experiencing a Sharp Rise in Dutch Red Sugar 120

Coarse Sand and White Sugar See Slight Stability

Yesterday, the sugar market happened to be Sunday, and there were no telegrams from the production area as usual. The coarse sand and white sugar atmosphere of the guild was slightly stable. Initially, the sellers asked for eight taels, but the buyers were unusually quiet. Only retail investors had a slight intention to buy, and the transaction price was seven taels and nine and a half qian, with no rise or fall compared to the previous day. No. 20 medium sand white sugar was seven taels and eight and a half qian, and the transaction was very balanced. Dutch red sugar transactions were quite brisk, and the market saw a gradual increase. No. 10 goods were priced at six taels six qian to six qian and a half, and No. 12 goods were six taels and seven and a half qian, up to eight qian. The market was also very beautiful. Japan Sugar Minghua YRO mark was one tael and one qian and a half, YT mark was eight taels and three qian and a half, and YP mark was eight taels and five qian and a half. Transactions were active. Later, the sellers called for five points higher, and the buyers were few. Only YP mark was traded at eight taels and six qian. The market image was firm and stable. The whole Cuban Ocean was quoted at seven taels and two qian, and there was no transaction. There is a rumor that the factory ice has risen in price. There is a lot of water in the slag ice market, and the price of the market stock has followed the increase, with some calling for up to twelve taels, but there is little hope of a transaction. Ju Delong & Co. sold more than 6,400 bags of No. 2 Xiao Lüqing, priced at seven taels and one qian, which was also quite firm.

Prepare for Cooperation Movement Propaganda Week 122

Meeting Held Yesterday to Appoint Responsible Personnel

Propaganda Week Outline Plan Approved

July 5th is the World Cooperation Movement Memorial Day. The Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Government of this city have received orders from the Central Party Department and the National Government to hold a large-scale Cooperation Movement Propaganda Week from that date. After mutual consultation, it was decided that six agencies, including the Municipal Government, the Propaganda Department of the Municipal Party Department, the Civil Training Committee of the Municipal Party Department, the Training Department of the Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Government's Social Bureau, and the Municipal Government's Education Bureau, would jointly prepare everything. Yesterday morning at 10:00, the six agencies convened the first preparatory committee meeting in the meeting room of the Municipal Party Department. More than ten people, including Municipal Government representatives Chen Kecheng and Chen Xunyu, Municipal Propaganda Department Bao Rong and Xu Xingchu, Municipal Training Department Wu Xianren and Cai Bubai, Civil Training Committee Li Zheng, Municipal Social Bureau Ju Minggang and Gu Bingyuan, and representatives from various agencies, publicly elected Xu Xingchu as the chairman to preside over the meeting, which began with formal rituals. First, the chairman reported briefly, stating that the cooperation movement is one of the seven movements stipulated by the Central Government. Now that the people's livelihood is declining, it is even more necessary to strive to promote it. This time, the Central Government issued a general order to all provinces and cities across the country to unanimously hold a Cooperation Movement Propaganda Week from the World Cooperation Movement Day. This city should actively prepare and hold a large-scale Cooperation Movement Propaganda Week. The outline plan for the propaganda week has been drafted by the Municipal Propaganda Department. Please give your opinions to make it perfect. Then the motion was discussed: (1) The outline plan for the Cooperation Movement Propaganda Week in this city has been drafted, please approve it (Resolution) Modified and passed. News of the Labor Strike of French Concession Water and Electricity Workers Yesterday 126

The Labor's Attitude Is Resolute, Requesting Assistance from All Sectors

The Employer Still Has No Response, and the Strike Is Difficult to End Immediately

The labor strike of the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Union has been recorded in this newspaper. In recent days, the employer still has no response, and the attitude of all workers is extremely resolute. They hold meetings every day to discuss the negotiation policy. The news from yesterday is recorded as follows:

The police maintain order. Initially, the Public Security Bureau, not understanding the ins and outs of the case, often ordered the Second District and Liyuan Road police stations to prevent the meeting before receiving a notice from the Municipal Party Department. It has been heard that the Social Bureau has notified the Public Security Bureau that the union workers have a labor dispute, and the Social Bureau has summoned both parties for mediation, but the employer refused to attend and did not accept the mediation. Now they can only listen to the union meeting to discuss the method. Therefore, the police station in charge received this notice yesterday and sent police to the union to maintain order at any time. It is also learned that the union, in view of the strike period, is deeply afraid that reactionary elements will take the opportunity to incite workers and disrupt and sabotage the labor movement. It specifically sent a letter to the local Public Security Bureau police station to order the police chief to go to the union to strictly prevent this.

Re-requesting the mutual assistance of Chinese staff. The union previously sent a letter to all Chinese staff in the factory requesting unanimous assistance to the workers. For several days, the Chinese staff has not expressed anything. Yesterday, they sent another letter of persuasion, the original letter said: (Abbreviated above) Our union previously sent a letter requesting that you assist our union workers. I hope you can see clearly. However, for three days, there has been no clear indication, which is a loss of the spirit of love and mutual assistance among our Chinese compatriots. I still remember that you had intended to negotiate with the employer on a certain matter and had instructed our union workers to express mutual assistance. Although the matter was not carried out, the words are still in my ears. Then you and our union workers are not only in the same situation, but also have a considerable relationship of alliance in the historical process. How can you bear to sit idly by while our seven hundred workers are rejected by the employer and not lend a hand? Therefore, I send another letter requesting that you express your attitude immediately to assist our compatriots. The workers will be very fortunate, and our union will be very fortunate.

Requesting solidarity from all sectors. Yesterday, the union issued a letter requesting solidarity from party departments and unions at all levels in the city, as follows: All party departments and unions at all levels in the Shanghai Special Municipality are aware that imperialists are using all means to carry out economic aggression in China. They set up factories in China and let them fish for profits, hire our Chinese workers as their slaves, and exploit the meager wages earned by seven people's sweat and blood, leaving nothing behind and allowing them to be destroyed. The groans and pains of the workers are not taken care of. The workers of our union have recently been unable to maintain their lives due to the soaring rice prices, so they had to ask the employer to increase their wages to maintain their poor lives every day. The conditions put forward are all within the scope and have been announced in the newspaper long ago, and have been approved by the higher-level party department, and the Social Bureau has been approved to convene labor and management to mediate. However, on the day the Social Bureau convened mediation, the employer intentionally absented, and there is no doubt that they are oppressing the workers, despising the government, and despising the union. In anger, the workers of our union convened a members' meeting at any time and resolved to go on strike, hoping to promote the employer's awakening. Who knew that the capitalists of the imperialists would become even more intensified. When the workers entered the factory on the second day, a few workers were expelled and the iron gate was closed, refusing to allow them to enter the factory, regarding the workers as meat on the chopping block or worse. The workers of our union are in this environment of oppression. In fact, there is no need to strike, and it has become a strike phenomenon. It is necessary to know that this strike is purely the creation of the imperialist employers. Our seven hundred workers are already like walking on thin ice, like being on the edge of a deep abyss, in extreme danger. I hope that party departments and unions at all levels will unanimously support us, so that the imperialist capitalists can finally realize their mistakes and save our seven hundred workers from fire and water. I am deeply and urgently praying for this.

Steamboat and Timber Industry Workers Go on Strike 127

The steamboat and timber industry workers in this city, totaling more than 2,000 people, have recently demanded an increase in rice subsidies of six yuan per person per month due to high rice prices and expensive firewood, but the steamboat companies and contractors have not responded. Soldiers Must Have Car Passes to Take the Train 128

The General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force issued a notice yesterday and posted it at various stations, saying: For the sake of issuing a notice, it has been found that soldiers taking the train on official business have always been issued Type A and B car passes by the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs to show preferential treatment. However, recently, soldiers taking the train often do not use these car passes, but instead use passports or notes to force their way onto the train. If this is not strictly prohibited, it will not only affect the income of the Railway Bureau, but also greatly hinder military discipline. In the future, soldiers taking the train on official business must uniformly hold Type A and B car passes and may not use passports or notes instead. If anyone dares to violate this deliberately, once found, in addition to being ordered to make up the ticket according to the railway regulations, they shall also be severely punished. This notice is hereby issued. All soldiers taking the train must comply and not violate it. Sincerely, sincerely.

Statistics on Foreign Trade in this Port 129

Imported Goods Plummet

Exported Goods Show Minimal Increase

Recently, the foreign trade of this port, both imports and exports, has been greatly affected by the gold and silver market, with imports experiencing the most significant decline. According to investigations, the total value of imported goods in this port for May was 42,000,000 Haikwan Taels, while exports amounted to 36,000,000 Taels. The total figures from January to May show imports at 247,000,000 Taels and exports at 197,000,000 Taels. In comparison, the total value of imported goods during the same period last year was 274,000,000 Haikwan Taels, and exports totaled 190,000,000 Taels. Comparing the two periods, imports have decreased by as much as 27,000,000 Taels.

Page 14

While exports have increased by 7,000,000 Taels, the overall balance of imports and exports is far from satisfactory, showing a significant disparity.

Memorial Service for Fan ZhengLuo 131

Held Yesterday at the City Party Headquarters

The late Kuomintang member, Martyr Fan ZhengLuo, was murdered along with his relatives and friends at his residence in the Hehefang area of Avenue Joffre last November 11th, causing a great stir at the time. All parties expressed their grief. Subsequently, Liu Jiwu, Zhu Jiarang, Yi Zuanren, Cai Zhiqing, Wang Doyan, Chen Kecheng, Zhu Yingpeng, Fan Ningshu, Wang Xingyong, Xiao Jinfan, Chen Baolian, Feng Zhiyou, Gao Yunlu, Gu Zhenzhong, and Liu Tianpeng, friends and relatives of the deceased during his lifetime, initiated a memorial service, which was held yesterday on the third floor of the City Party Headquarters. Over 500 people attended. The preparatory committee, consisting of Zhu Yingpeng, Chen Kecheng, and Xiao Jinfan, presided over the meeting, with Zhu Jiarang as the recorder and Yi Zuanren as the master of ceremonies. Other members of the preparatory committee served as ushers. Chairman Chen Kecheng reported, stating briefly, "Comrade Fan ZhengLuo was murdered last November 11th, causing great grief to comrades throughout the city and compatriots from all walks of life. Today, as we commemorate Comrade Fan ZhengLuo, we should consider three aspects: first, recall the situation during Comrade Fan's lifetime; second, recall the circumstances of his death; and third, express our feelings of grief. Because I, as a brother, worked with the deceased for a long time, I am more familiar with the various circumstances and can report a few points. Comrade Fan was very brave from a young age. Since leaving school, he followed Comrade Zhengbo in the revolution, demonstrating his brave spirit everywhere. When he was in the investigation section of the city's training department, where I was also in charge, the reactionary forces of the communists outside the party were very rampant. Other comrades with less courage were often intimidated by this, but Comrade Fan often said to me that the responsibility of our investigation section was to investigate corruption within the party.

Deterioration, and to resolutely restrain anti-party forces outside the party. Therefore, whenever the reactionaries took any action, Comrade Fan would report it to other comrades or make his own determination. However, Comrade Fan later felt that although his work within the party was very active, his inability to take direct action to restrain the reactionaries was a regret. Therefore, he resolutely transferred to the Public Security Bureau, thinking to do more practical work. Since joining the bureau, he, of course, fulfilled his long-cherished aspirations, and he went forward bravely and freely, eliminating reactionaries, always expressing his brave spirit, resolute and decisive attitude, and determination to struggle and sacrifice. But very sadly, at a time when society and the country needed this kind of talent, his strong suppression in peacetime provoked the jealousy of the reactionaries. Of course, the reactionaries' plan was not directed at him alone, but Comrade Fan ZhengLuo was eventually sacrificed, and this is how painful it is for us. Secondly, we think about the circumstances of Comrade Fan's death. Although I was not at the scene at the time, I heard from Comrade Zhengbo and others afterwards that a guest had come to his house that night, and just as the guest was about to leave and Comrade Zhengbo was about to see him off, the communist bandits had already ambushed at the door. At that time, Comrade ZhengLuo was behind, just leaving the door, when he suddenly heard two loud bangs. Knowing there was a change, he rushed out to resist the reactionaries, but in the end, he was killed by the enemy's malicious bullets, groaning in the middle of a pool of blood and died. We think if he was not brave, this would not have happened, because he was very brave and sacrificed himself. We are very sad about the death of Comrade Fan, but we have not had the opportunity to vent to the public since last November 12th. Although everyone often talks about it among friends, everyone is saddened, and even when eating and sleeping, we often remember Comrade Fan's life, the happy situation of gathering together. Comrade Fan took the revolution as his second life. He never talked about boring things or did boring things. He not only preached revolution, but also practiced it. His revolution has had real achievements, but he also did not always publicize or exaggerate to everyone, which is his virtue and what we, the surviving revolutionary comrades, should strive to do. Comrade Fan ZhengLuo sacrificed for the revolution. We, the surviving comrades, are gathered here today, feeling very sad. On the one hand, we mourn the misfortune of the party, the country, and society, the loss of such a revolutionary activist, and on the other hand, we feel that our responsibility is even greater. We should not shirk this responsibility. We should find an opportunity to avenge Comrade Fan and complete the unfinished business of Comrade Fan," and so on. The following is a summary of the speeches of the attendees: (1) Chen Dezheng, Executive Committee Member of the City, said, "It is comforting from the perspective of the deceased that he sacrificed his life for righteousness, because Comrade ZhengLuo's strength lies in his spirited, courageous, and uncompromising spirit, and his fearlessness of death. Therefore, sacrificing his life for righteousness was almost within his expectations. We who are his friends cannot avoid being saddened in terms of human feelings, but at this time of rampant reaction, we should rise up and take it as our responsibility to eliminate the reactionaries." (2) Yu Hongjun, representative of the mayor, said, "Comrade Fan was a capable and intelligent talent of our party, and especially his uncompromising, resolute, and brave spirit has always been admired. Now that he has given his life for the party, we have a hundred feelings and are extremely saddened. Fortunately, all comrades will continue his spirit from now on to complete his unfinished will." (3) Yuan Liang, Director of the Public Security Bureau, said, "Comrade Fan came to the Public Security Bureau to handle affairs. I saw his brave spirit at his home and asked him to come. Not long after he started, his spirit was fully expressed. Everyone is very sad today at the memorial service, but I feel that the Public Security Bureau has lost a good helper in the future and feels more responsible. In the future, I will work harder under the leadership of the party to eliminate the rebels to repay the party and the country and to comfort Comrade Fan's spirit under the spring." (4) Tao Baichuan, Executive Committee Member of the City, said, "Today, Comrade Fan's friends are holding a memorial service, but in a few days, the City Party Headquarters will also hold a larger memorial service to express their condolences. Comrade Fan has many strengths, and his brave spirit is most admirable. Today, the voices of reaction outside the party have not subsided, and it is even sadder to come to commemorate Comrade Fan." (5) Wei Bokuan, Executive Committee Member of the City, said, "We learn two lessons from Comrade Fan's murder: First, the concession has no guarantee for the lives of Chinese people, and it should be taken back as soon as possible. Second, we must not be lenient with the reactionaries' ruthless methods." (6) Pan Gongzhan, Executive Committee Member of the City, said, "The Communist Party's reactionaries never talk about benevolence and righteousness. They have no motherland or race, only class. They are so ruthless to people of the same race, which is hateful. We should deeply recognize this in the future and must not be lenient when dealing with them. We must know that the Prime Minister's spirit of generosity and fraternity must not be thrown at them." (7) Liu Tianpeng, a member of the preparatory committee, said in his speech, "To commemorate Comrade Fan, we should recognize his spirit from his words and deeds and continue his will." The French police have not arrested the murderer yet, and we should urge them to solve the case as soon as possible. Fan Zhengbo, a member of the family, gave a reply, stating briefly, "I am too sad today to report, please forgive me," and said with tears in her voice, and the whole audience was silent. The attached eulogy said, "You lived as a hero of the party and died as a martyr of the party. You struggled for the revolution throughout your life and were attacked by villains. You have no regrets in becoming a martyr. The hot blood of a man can be seen by the Prime Minister's spirit in heaven and can inspire those who die after. Thinking of the stealth of the murderers, knowing the stubbornness and cunning of the imperialists, and now the thieves of the marshes are raising the mausoleums and stealing the treasures. The vast Central Plains is covered by haze. If you have knowledge underground, you should not close your eyes and believe in the ultimate victory of the doctrine, destroy all the remnants of reaction, and store the great flag of Qingbai to lay the party and the country on a solid rock, so that the heroic spirits should be in Jiuyuan. I hereby announce its arrival, Shangxiang."

Liu Zuhan's Talk 132

Liu Zuhan, the newly appointed commander of the Jiangbei Guerrilla Forces by the Central Government, was sworn in at the Pingjiang Public Office in Zhabei on the 19th. The reporter specially visited Liu at his residence on Luban Road in the French Concession the day before yesterday, asking when he would go to Jiangbei in person, where the headquarters would be set up, and what the organizational structure would be. Liu answered one by one (the following are all in Liu's words): "I originally intended to set off immediately after taking office this time, but the deployment of tickets has not been fully prepared, and it will be delayed by about one star before I can set off. The headquarters will be temporarily set up in Yangzhou. As for all the organizational structures, I cannot predict them at the moment, because the army in Jiangbei is extremely complex, and there are many gangs of bandits. I intend to use both suppression and appeasement. Therefore, since the announcement of my appointment, there must be several people a day who have returned to allegiance. However, in order to prevent someone from making a statement in disguise outside, I absolutely do not appoint a single person in Shanghai. After I arrive in Jiangbei, I must conduct a detailed and careful review one by one, and then engage in compilation, before I can have a concrete grasp." After speaking, visitors came in an endless stream, and the reporter resigned.

Ninth District Party Headquarters

Opposing the Violation of Treaty Rights by Western Consuls 133

The National Society said, "The Ninth District Party Headquarters of this city, in order to oppose the destruction of treaties and infringement of legal rights by the Spanish Consul, issued a declaration, the original text of which reads, "Yesterday, it was reported in the newspapers that the Russian merchant Robin Foreign Company of this city accused the Spanish Wangdetang Mayor of a case. When the court summoned him in the special district court, the defendant deliberately failed to appear, which was obviously contemptuous of Chinese laws and regulations. He should have been summoned and detained. Originally, in order to uphold the relationship between the two countries, he was treated with leniency, but he did not realize it and was protested by the Spanish Consul, which suspended the trial. It was found that Article 2 of the Sino-Spanish Treaty of Amity and Commerce, signed in Nanjing on December 27, 17th year of the Republic of China, detailed, "The people of this contracting state shall be subject to the laws and courts of the other contracting state within the territory of the other contracting state, but for the exercise and defense of their rights, they shall have the freedom and convenience to petition the courts." There is also an official statement from Spanish country China Minister Youlide to our country at the same time, stating that the Spanish government fully agrees to all of Article 2 of the Sino-Spanish Treaty of Amity and Commerce signed and will take effect on January 1, 19th year of the Republic of China, which is on file. Now, suddenly, in accordance with the abolished consular jurisdiction, it obstructs the progress of the court's trial, violates the treaty, and damages the country's reputation and credit. Especially, it infringes on our country's exercise of legal rights and jurisdiction. The court can legally reject its unreasonable protest and dispose of the default judgment to show the majesty of our country's laws and prevent future occurrences. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs should make a serious protest and warn it to abide by the credit of the treaty in order to maintain the friendship between China and Spain. If the court believes that a diplomatic incident has occurred and considers it important, and the case is suspended invisibly, it will not only lose the exercise of legal rights within the territory, but also leave foreigners saying that we are weak and incompetent, and the future of the judiciary will have one more hidden reef. The people of the country should pay attention together, not be taken advantage of by foreigners, and urge the party authorities to resist according to law, so as not to fall into an irrecoverable situation. This is a declaration."

The Relief Association Receives Medicines from the War Zone 134

Dispatching Personnel Today to Distribute Them

The Relief Association was ordered to handle the compensation for the Guide war zone. It has published advertisements to solicit medicines, and various sectors have donated a large number of medicines such as Sha medicine water, Changchun Pills, and Tianzhong Tea. They have all been collected by the Shanghai Office. In particular, Susheng Pharmaceutical Company donated 1,000 packs of hemostatic cotton, which is effective in hemostasis and will be especially useful in the war zone. Now, Xu Jingren, Chairman of the Association, has appointed Zhang Shien as a special commissioner to go to Guide to handle compensation matters. He will have to leave within days. He specifically telegraphed Wang Yiting of the Shanghai Office yesterday, asking him to send the received relief medicines and other items to Beijing as soon as possible so that they can be handed over to Special Commissioner Zhang to carry and distribute. After receiving the telegram, the office sent it for inspection and dispatched the car to pack it separately. It is approved to send people to the meeting by car tonight. If any sectors are willing to help with the war zone's medicine, please send it to the Shanghai Office of the Association in Renji Hall, Yunnan Road, today, and it can still be brought to Beijing.

Jishi Society

Disaster Relief for the Jinan Arsenal Explosion 135

The Chinese Jishi Society recently received a telegram from Zhou Junjingfu, the director of the Beiping Relief Office, a telegram from She Guisheng Yuan, the director of the Tianjin Relief Office, and an urgent telegram from Shen Baoying and others, saying that the Jinan Daming Lake Arsenal exploded, causing many deaths and injuries in more than 20 streets, the situation is extremely miserable, please ask your association for relief, etc. The association is currently running out of funds for relief in various provinces and cannot cope with it. It has replied by letter and has recently received another letter from the two directors, Zhou and She, reporting that the disaster in the Jinan Arsenal explosion is so miserable that it cannot bear to see it. No one is providing relief at this time, and the people cannot live. Please try to raise emergency relief to save the rest of the people. The association could not bear to abandon it but could not afford to do it, and had no choice but to raise 5,000 yuan in relief funds, and wired it to Director She, and allocated it to Director Zhou, to personally go to the disaster to temporarily save the rare disaster in case of emergency.

There is also news from this city transferred to the back page

Page 15

News of Brave Students in This City

Escaping from a Bandit Den by Shooting 148

An Old Wet Nurse with Sinister Intentions

A Honey Trap in a Circus

Wang Changyan Imprisoned in the East Wing

Seizing a Gun and Frightening Away a Gang of Bandits

Gu Yin Wang Mao, a military man. When Wang Zhanyuan was Governor of Hubei, he served as the commander of the 18th Division. After Wang's defeat, he retired to his hometown, enjoying his life in seclusion, like a feudal lord. His second son, Changyan, is married and 23 years old. He has been studying law in Shanghai for many years and will graduate this summer and return home. However, due to an occasional indiscretion, he ended up in a bandit den and narrowly escaped disaster. The one who lured and kidnapped him was the wet nurse, Wang, who had served him for many years. Wang was kidnapped at 10:00 PM the night before last night and escaped at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon. Although he was in the hands of the bandits for less than 20 hours, his experiences before and after were fantastic, making it an interesting case among the kidnapping cases in Shanghai. The details are as follows:

The Young Master Meets the Wet Nurse. Wang Changyan studies at the local School of Political Science and Law, commuting from his rented dormitory at No. 270, Xinxin Lane, Jin Shenfu Road. Four weeks ago, while strolling in the Great World, he suddenly met his wet nurse, Pan Jinmei. The master and servant met unexpectedly. Pan introduced herself to Wang, calling him Young Master and asking how he was living in Shanghai. Wang replied that he was studying at school and would graduate soon and return to Ningbo. Pan repeatedly agreed and said that she now lived at No. 407, Shanhai Guan Road, and would be happy to be at his service if needed.

Occasional Visits Lead to Meeting a Man. After meeting Aunt Pan, Wang often sent clothes to her for washing, about three or four times. Each time, he met a man who claimed to be Gao Shaogu, a close relative according to Aunt Pan, but actually her lover. Because of his relationship with the wet nurse, Wang often used gentle language. The day before yesterday evening, Wang went again and told Pan that he had nothing to do in Shanghai and was packing his luggage to return to Ningbo the next day. He asked if she would like to visit the old house again. Pan replied that she was afraid of traveling by sea and could not serve the young master. Gao, who was also present, suddenly said to Wang that if he could set off on Monday (today), the matter would be settled because he also wanted to return to his hometown to visit relatives. Gao was from Cixi. Wang nodded, thinking that staying in Shanghai for another day or two would not hurt.

The Three Go to the Circus. Gao heard Wang's words and postponed his departure, seemingly overjoyed, saying that staying in Shanghai for two more days would be a great opportunity for sightseeing. He said that the circus performance in the newspaper was amazing and worth seeing, but he was always busy and had no time to enjoy it. The circus was performing at the intersection of Carter Road. Wang had often passed by Pan's house and had long wanted to go. Hearing Gao's words, he was immediately excited and said that if the wet nurse and Gao were willing, they should go. So the three of them went to the circus.

A Beautifully Dressed Woman Is Met in the Circus. Wang, Aunt Pan, and Gao entered the circus and found seats. Suddenly, they saw a smiling woman nearby. Pan greeted her, saying, "You are here too?" Her tone suggested that it was an unexpected encounter, but it was actually a lure. She introduced Wang to the woman, and Pan told Wang about the woman and praised her beauty. After the show, as they were leaving, Pan tugged at Wang's sleeve and said that the woman's residence was not far away and it was not yet late, so why not visit her house. Gao also encouraged him to go. Wang did not say anything, nor did he refuse. So they hired rickshaws and went to Gengqing Lane, Xinzha Road.

Upon Entering the Room, the Situation Becomes Tense. When they arrived at Gengqing Lane, it was around 10:00 PM. The residence was at No. 689, and the alley was clean, not like a place where vulgar people would live, so Wang felt at ease and was calm. Then, they went upstairs into the east wing. Wang suddenly saw three or four burly men in the room, and the furnishings did not seem like those of good people. Wang began to suspect something. When he heard the people in the room speak, he almost screamed in panic, but a gun was already pointed at his chest. Wang knew that if he made a sound, he would be in danger, so he tried to stay calm and observe the situation, but nothing happened. They only told him to stay put and be quiet.

Four Burly Men Share the Bed. Wang had been sleeping alone in his dormitory for a long time. That night, there were suddenly four men in the room, sharing the bed with him, which made him uncomfortable. He tossed and turned all night and could not fall asleep. He occasionally heard the guards talking, but he could not understand much. He knew that he had been sold by Aunt Pan. Fortunately, the four men were tired in the morning, and two other burly men replaced them. Wang knew that even if he had wings, he could not fly away, and he saw that they all had weapons on their waists, so he dared not even think about it.

A Plan Is Conceived When Feigning Sleep. The food served at noon was not bad. After the meal, Wang leaned on the couch and pretended to be asleep. One of the bandits went downstairs, leaving only one person in the room, pacing around the bed, guarding him closely. Wang suddenly had an idea and pretended to go to sleep. He closed his eyes tightly, pretending to be fast asleep, and snoring in his throat, as if he were sleeping soundly. The bandit thought that it was normal to take a nap after a meal and seemed to relax a bit. Suddenly, Wang felt a strong urge to urinate. He did not have time to leave the room, so he used the spittoon next to the small couch Wang was lying on. Although his movements were very light, Wang heard it clearly.

Eyes Quickly Seize Gun and Fire. Because of his need to relieve himself, the bandit took the gun from his waist and placed it on the edge of the bed. Wang quickly jumped up, but the bandit was immediately alerted. He quickly abandoned the spittoon and rushed out the door. Wang held the gun in his hand and shot at him, firing three shots. The bandits downstairs heard the alarm and ran back upstairs, firing at Wang. Fortunately, they could not hit him in their haste, and Wang was unharmed. He shouted for help loudly and urgently. The bandits were terrified and ran downstairs, escaping with a female bandit, said to be Wang's wet nurse, Pan Jinmei.

Bandits Return Fire and Wound a Woman. Wang's cries for help and the sound of gunfire were heard outside. The Indian police guarding the alley immediately closed the gate and rushed to the police station to report the emergency. However, they did not know the details and only reported a theft. The Gordon Road Police Station immediately dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives, who arrived very quickly. However, the bandits had already taken advantage of this very short opportunity to escape from the back door opposite No. 689, firing their guns as a warning. A woman was wounded by a stray bullet, and the bandits escaped without a trace.

Traces of Blood on the Stairs. When the Chinese and foreign detectives from the Gordon Road Police Station arrived at the scene, they found several shell casings scattered on the ground, and there were also traces of blood on the stairs, suggesting that one of the bandits had been injured before escaping. When they entered the east wing, Wang had already raised his hands in surrender, and the gun he used to shoot the bandits was lying on the table. The detectives saw that Wang was about twenty years old, wearing a blue silk gown, looking thin with a hint of panic on his face. When they questioned him, they found that he was a student. The detectives were amazed when they heard his story of how he had escaped by shooting the bandits.

The Landlord Talks About Renting the House. Although the bandits who kidnapped Wang had escaped, the police were making every effort to investigate. It was said that the bandits had gone to rent the house on the 19th and moved in the next morning with their family and household items, which were not too frugal. The landlord did not suspect anything. The only slightly different thing was that more men came and went, but they were not visiting relatives or friends, and there were some suspicious things when they went upstairs. No one but the bandits knew that Wang Changyan was imprisoned in the east wing. Their tactics were extraordinary.

First Five Months of the Year

Shanghai's Foreign Trade 149

Pessimistic Information Predominates

Both Imports and Exports Are Sluggish

According to the Japanese Deputy Consul in Shanghai, Kato, the total foreign trade volume of Shanghai from January to May this year, imports were about 247 million Haikwan taels, and exports were about 197 million Haikwan taels, compared with the import volume of 274 million taels and the export volume of 190 million taels in the same period last year. Imports decreased by 27 million taels, and exports increased by 7 million taels. It is worth noting that the import of rice this year is much higher than in previous years, indicating that the import of general goods is much less than last year. The decrease in imports after April is due to the implementation of gold import duties starting from February 1st, especially the increase in the conversion rate starting from March 16th. More imports were made in the first two or three months, which led to a decrease in imports in April and May. In addition, poor harvests, deteriorating political situation, interrupted inland transportation, rampant bandits, and the concentration of silver dollars in Shanghai led to financial obstruction in the interior, drastic changes in exchange rates, and the impact of low prices in Japan. These are also the reasons for the sluggish imports. On the export side, due to the low silver price, operations are profitable, and there has been a slight increase since March and April. However, major items such as raw silk, tea, and cotton, although operations are profitable due to drastic changes in the silver price, the actual transactions are not as expected. However, the export of raw silk is less due to seasonal factors and scarce inventory. The export of fertilizers is also not prosperous due to the weak market conditions in Japan. As for other ports, Dalian and Qingdao are as usual, while Hankou and Tianjin are extremely sluggish due to the impact of the political situation. In short, China's foreign trade in the first half of this year is expected to decrease by 10% to 15% in imports compared with last year, and exports will increase slightly. The total imports and exports will decrease by about 10%.

Fewer Criminal Cases Last Week 150

The Shanghai Times reported that the number of criminals arrested by the Public Concession police last week was greatly reduced compared with the previous week, and the number of criminal cases was also less. There were only a few major cases. However, after several weeks of peace, armed robbery resumed its activities. There were reports of shops, residents, and pedestrians being robbed from time to time. A total of six robbery suspects were arrested this week. All of them were found to have guns when they were arrested. Two of them have been identified as repeat offenders. A total of seven pickpockets were arrested, all of whom were repeat offenders. Twelve robbers were arrested, eight of whom were also repeat offenders.

Timber Boat Lost at Sea 151

Investigation Reveals It Was Dismantled by Nanhui Residents

The timber boat Jin Wanfeng, loaded with various timber worth more than 10,000 taels from Fujian, arrived at the Lihong pier in Wusong last month. The boat suddenly leaked and could not move forward. The crew members, fearing that the boat would sink, took small boats to escape ashore and reported to the boat owner, who hired a tugboat to tow the boat, but the boat had disappeared. After investigation, the boat owner found out that the timber boat had drifted to the Wutuan sea area in Nanhui County due to the wind. The nearby residents saw that it was a drifting timber boat and no one came to claim it, so they robbed all the timber and completely dismantled the boat. The Fuzhou Liangzhe Timber Merchants Association learned that the boat had encountered danger and, according to the law, anyone must protect it. Now, both the boat and the goods have been robbed and dismantled, with a loss of about 20,000 gold. The residents of that area have no regard for the law. A letter was sent to the Wusong Chamber of Commerce a few days ago to investigate the truth and provide assistance. After receiving the letter, the Wusong Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Nanhui County Government yesterday, requesting a thorough investigation, strict punishment according to the law, and compensation for the goods to protect shipping merchants and warn against similar acts.

The houses in the Chungeng Lane area of the Public Concession's West Chessboard Street, east to Henan Road, west to Shandong Road, south to Avenue Edward VII, and north to Jinlong Street, including municipal houses, number in the hundreds and are owned by Zhou Weishi. Nanshi and Pudong

Rice Boat

Dispute Over Mid-Journey Inspections 156

Rice boat owners from the South Bund, including Ding Jisheng and others, recently transported rice to Shanghai. While passing Bridge No. 34 on the Shanghai-Hangzhou railway line, they were suddenly ordered to stop by the stationed troops for inspection. After the inspection, they were forced to dock and were not allowed to proceed immediately. Ding argued, leading to him being beaten and injured. After the rice boats arrived in Shanghai and unloaded, most were unwilling to return to the interior for more cargo. The South Bund Rice Merchants Association sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, requesting them to forward the message to the relevant military authorities, ordering the troops stationed there to cancel inspections of rice boats passing through. Now, the rice merchants in the interior have loaded rice onto boats, but hearing that the rice boats are unwilling to transport it, they have sent representatives to Shanghai to request the Chamber of Commerce to petition the government to promptly cancel the inspections, so that rice boats can resume normal transport. At yesterday's Chamber of Commerce meeting, Chairman Yan reported that Ding Jisheng's boats and others were transporting rice to Shanghai when, while passing Bridge No. 34, they were suddenly ordered to stop by the stationed troops, who insisted on inspecting the boats. Ding argued, leading to him being beaten and injured. The boats were detained for a day before being released. Rice boats in Shanghai, hearing this, were alarmed and dared not return to load cargo. Consequently, many rice boats behind Ding's were turned back to the interior, afraid to pass through. The Chamber of Commerce had sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, requesting them to forward the message to the relevant military authorities, ordering the troops stationed there to cancel inspections of rice boats passing through. However, rice boats recently arriving in Shanghai reported that although they saw stationed troops while passing Bridge No. 34, they were not ordered to stop for inspection. It is believed that this matter arose from a misunderstanding. Currently, rice boats are passing through as usual. Please inform the rice businesses in the interior so that the rice boats will no longer be alarmed. Also, inform the rice boats in Shanghai to return to the interior to load cargo as soon as possible, and ask rice dealers to inform the rice businesses in the interior.

Smuggling Soldiers Sell Smuggled Salt 166

Knowingly Commit the Crime, Sentenced to Six Months in Prison

Chen Deguang, a soldier of the current rank in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces' Anti-Smuggling Team, from northern Jiangsu, would hide the smuggled salt he seized without reporting it to the authorities and sell it privately. This kind of private profit-seeking behavior is more harmful than that of smugglers because it allows smuggled salt to flood the market, causing official sales to decline. At 2:00 PM on Friday, the 5th, Chen carried a load of smuggled salt, weighing 130 catties, produced in Pudong, and sold it in the Yangshupu area. While passing Linqing Road, he was spotted by a Chinese police officer from the 218th Third Pier. Because the salt bags were black and light and did not have the whiteness of official salt, he questioned him. Chen's answer was evasive. The police officer arrested the man and the salt and notified the Gongmao Salt Shop to send someone to the police station to confirm that it was indeed smuggled salt. The next morning, he was sent to the Special District Court. Jiang Baoli, a lawyer from the salt shop, argued in court that the defendant was a soldier in the Anti-Smuggling Team who sold smuggled salt, knowingly committing the crime, and should be severely punished. According to Chen, the salt was transported from Yuyao. After questioning, Judge Ge sentenced Chen Deguang to six months in prison and confiscated the smuggled salt.

Zhang Lianying's testimony was the same. The Chinese and Western officials sentenced Wu A'gen and Zhang Lianying each to two months in prison, suspended for three years.

Two Yancheng Natives Assault 171

Each Fined Thirty Dollars

Wang Wanhe and Wang Wanyin, natives of Jiancheng, had a verbal argument with a woman surnamed Liu from the same village on Guangxin Road. Wang Wanhe slapped her in the face, knocking her to the ground, and Wang Wanyin stabbed her hands and legs with a knife. Fortunately, the injuries were minor, and she recovered the next day. The two Wangs fled at the time but were later arrested by the police. At first, they denied the assault. The day before yesterday, the police summoned witnesses and transferred them to the Special District Court. After questioning by Judge Ge, the two Wangs were sentenced to a fine of thirty dollars each. If they were unable to pay, they would be imprisoned for one day for every two dollars.

Robbers Each Sentenced to Four Years 172

Six robbers suddenly came to the home of Chen Liansheng at No. 568 Fangbanqiao North, MinGuo Road in the French Concession. Three of them, armed with guns, went inside and robbed them of their clothing and silver before fleeing. The victims sounded the alarm, and the police arrived and arrested two of the robbers, Ren Guixiang and Wang San, and took them to the police station. The day before yesterday, they were sent to the French Court for investigation. First, the plaintiffs filed a complaint about the robbery. The two robbers, Ren and Wang, confessed to organizing the robbery with accomplices. The Chinese and Western officials sentenced the two defendants to four years each in the Western Prison and ordered them to be permanently expelled from the Concession after their sentences were completed.

Accusation of Theft by a Russian Found to Have No Evidence 173

Zhang Weizu, residing at No. 648 Xiafei Road in the French Concession and working as an accountant at Huiyuan Trust Company, filed a complaint with the Criminal Court of the French Court the day before yesterday, stating that the businessman was returning home from the company yesterday and took a tram on the Bund. At the intersection of Dama Road, a Russian named Pang Deng and his friend boarded the tram and sat with the businessman. They pretended to read the newspaper, covering his face. He then felt someone probing his pocket. The businessman had five hundred dollars in his pocket. He immediately checked the money and found that one hundred dollars was missing. Pang's friend got off the tram and left. The businessman reported to the police officer on duty and arrested Pang, requesting an investigation. The defendant, Pang Deng, was represented by lawyer Puleimei, who stated that the defendant was in the jewelry business and had a good reputation. He was also taking the tram home that day and was falsely accused of theft by the plaintiff. The accusation was without evidence and requested that it be dismissed and that he be allowed to file a counterclaim for damages to his reputation. Judge Zhu ruled that the plaintiff's accusation was without evidence and should be dismissed.

Strict Prohibition of Dragon Flags 179

The Shanghai County Government recently received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, which forwarded instructions from the Ministry of Interior, stating that it has recently been found that in various places, villagers still use the dragon flag of the former Qing Dynasty during deity worship gatherings, waving them conspicuously in parades, acting as if they were not doing anything wrong. Although this is due to the ignorance and lack of knowledge of the villagers, it forms a reactionary movement. Under the clear sky and white sun, such imperial dragon flags should not be allowed to exist. The county magistrate was instructed to strictly prohibit the use of dragon flags and destroy them to maintain the system. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Yan yesterday forwarded the order to the County Public Security Bureau, instructing all branch offices to comply and strictly prohibit and destroy dragon flags at any time to maintain the system.

Letters to the Editor 183

To the esteemed Chief Editor,

Greetings. On May 20th, a dead body was found floating on the East China Sea. The face was no longer clear. The person was approximately fifty years old, had a jade bracelet on his hand, and had nearly twenty yuan in cash in his clothing (this amount has been used). There were also five or six cards bearing the name Chen Shanfu, a native of Nanhai, Guangdong. We previously sent a letter to the Guangdong Guild Hall, but we have now heard that there is no such guild hall in Shanghai, or perhaps the name is slightly different. We respectfully request that your newspaper publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section so that his family can claim the body. This would be a truly virtuous act. With this, I wish you peace.

Respectfully submitted by villager Zhu Jinqi on June 17th.

Regarding the news item in your newspaper's local news column, "Mother and Son Dispute Property," which stated that Ningbo native Yu Longzhang recently claimed that after the death of his father, Yu Jinlin, the entire estate was seized by his father's concubine, Yu Cai, etc. (details omitted), we are extremely shocked. According to our client, Yu Cai, she is Yu Jinlin's second wife, and her memorial tablet has already been placed in the Yu clan's ancestral hall and recorded in the genealogy, with conclusive evidence. Furthermore, when Yu Cai married Yu Jinlin in 1915, Yu Longzhang was only five years old and was raised by Yu Cai. From childhood to adulthood and marriage, he always called Yu Cai "Mother." Even in the recent reports, Yu Longzhang claimed to be in mourning at the behest of his late mother, clearly acknowledging Yu Cai as his mother. Unexpectedly, Yu Longzhang falsely accused Yu Cai of being Yu Jinlin's mistress from his early years and not his second wife. Yu Cai has filed a criminal lawsuit with the local court against him for intentionally damaging her reputation, and the case is currently under review. We request that this letter be published. Respectfully submitted by Lawyer Dai Chengxiang on June 22, 1930.

Special Publication

Tang Weizhi Urges Immediate Action to Relieve the Rice Shortage 184

Whenever I hear about the suffering of the people in recent times, I feel heartbroken and cannot restrain myself. Today, the rice shortage is an urgent problem. The more expensive rice becomes, the more difficult life becomes for the people. The more difficult life becomes for the people, the more bandits there will be. In recent years, various provinces have experienced famine, and most of the relief has been provided by Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. However, in the near future, the counties north of the Yangtze River will likely become like Shaanxi and Gansu. If the essence of southeastern Zhejiang is exhausted, the national economy and the people's livelihood will also be exhausted with it. Moreover, with continuous rain, if we encounter a disaster this year, there will inevitably be starving people everywhere. How can we, the poor people, bear this? Thinking of this, I want to cry but have no tears.

The most urgent measure to address the root cause of the problem is to request that the Shanghai public-spirited merchants and the public-spirited merchants in the interior, as well as the public-spirited rice merchants in various places, jointly organize a Rice Shortage Relief Association. All the public funds accumulated in various counties should be investigated and allocated. Those without cash should be asked to donate as much as possible and purchase indica rice and flour in full quantities. They should be prepared for flat-rate sales and timed circulation until the new rice is harvested. If the above measures cannot be cooperated on for the time being, please ask each county to prepare separately and gradually promote them. All farmers' banks in various places are intended to facilitate farmers. The method is good, and the intention is beautiful. This matter should also imitate the community granary method, purchase rice and grain, and lend it to farmers, who will repay the principal later. This will further benefit the feelings of farmers. As for the rice merchants in various counties, if there are any goods in storage, please show great compassion and sell them quickly so that the market can circulate funds. If more rice is imported in this way, even those in various provinces who are begging for relief can also benefit from the surplus. (Yesterday, I saw a newspaper report about Jiangxi Province begging for relief, and the text was extremely painful.) If the rain does not stop and the new crops are submerged, farmers should be notified immediately to prepare to plant late rice and various grains as appropriate (they should be planted according to the products suitable for the local soil, and the priority should be given to those that are resistant to hunger) to make up for the losses.

The Book of Documents says, "They hold their wives and children in their arms and appeal to Heaven with sorrow." Mencius said, "If people suddenly see a child about to fall into a well, they will all feel alarmed and compassionate." Today, the rice shortage is so severe that many villagers are living on bean dregs and chaff. How can we bear to sit idly by and do nothing? As the saying goes, "It is difficult to buy poverty in times of difficulty with money." We urge benevolent gentlemen to quickly join forces to plan and maintain. At this time, being able to raise a few bushels of rice can extend the lives of several poor people. With tears streaming down my face, I present these words, hoping for your kind consideration.

Respectfully submitted by Tang Wenzhi.
