Art World

Nationalistic

Literary and Art Movement 185

Declaration of Publication

At the beginning of this month, those involved in the Nationalistic Literary and Art Movement gathered somewhere in this city and issued a declaration, attracting the attention of the literary and art circles. We have obtained the original text of the declaration and publish it below.

The Chinese Nationalist Literary and Art Movement held a meeting in Shanghai on June 1, 1930, and issued the following declaration:

(1)

China's literary and art circles have recently fallen deeply into a deformed and morbid developmental process. This phenomenon will not be denied by anyone who pays even slight attention to China's art and literary scene today. Today's current situation is precisely the crisis of Chinese literature and art.

If we take a look at our literary and art scene today, we can discover this mixed situation. We will see that in this new literary and artistic era, there are still people who maintain residual feudal thoughts. The history of China's New Literary and Art Movement is not very long. Although its acceptance by the general public cannot be denied, from the time the New Literary and Art Movement occurred until today, because those engaged in the New Literary and Art Movement lacked a central consciousness of literature and art, and focused on formal reforms while neglecting the enrichment of content, all residual feudal thoughts are still invisibly dominating everything. This is undeniable.

At the same time, we see the so-called proletarian literary and art movement that calls itself the left wing. They "present" art "to the bloody struggle of 'victory or death'" and "...art cannot but take as its content the feelings felt by the proletariat in this dark class society of the 'Middle Ages'..." At the same time, we also see the movement of the so-called left-wing painter association. In their declaration, they say, "Gentlemen, please look at those gold-worshipping painters. Apart from their own fame and gold, apart from their own territory and luxurious lives, they have never worked for our benefit... Young artists, you should recognize that their deception and exploitation are their consistent policies of oppression..." Therefore, in our China, the old literature and art have collapsed, but in the process of building new literature and art, this kind of conscious class art movement has emerged.

In such two extremes of thought, we can still see many forms of situations. Each small organization possesses a subjective view. Therefore, today's new literary and art scene in China is filled with fragmented remnants. In such a situation, a central consciousness of literature and art cannot be formed. Therefore, from the time of the New Literary and Art Movement until today, we have achieved very little in new literature and art. If this multi-faceted literary and artistic consciousness develops along its respective perceived path, then this chaotic remnant of literature and art will never disappear. The result will be that our New Literary and Art Movement will never have a chance to develop and will inevitably collapse. The current phenomenon is precisely the crisis of our new literature and art.

But how can we break through this crisis and allow our New Literary and Art Movement to evolve to a bright and glorious realm? First, we believe that the current crisis of Chinese literature and art is due to the multifaceted views on literature and art, and the lack of a central consciousness in the entire developmental process of new literature and art. Therefore, the only way to break through this current crisis is to strive for the formation of a central consciousness in the evolutionary process of new literature and art.

(2)

Art, from its earliest historical records, has clearly shown us the mission it bears. We understand very clearly that works of art in their original state are not produced from individual consciousness but from the consciousness of life formed from the standpoint of the nation. What is displayed in a work of art is not only the artist's talent, technique, style, and form. At the same time, what is displayed in a work of art is also the product of the nation to which the artist belongs. This is very clearly told to us in the name of art.

From the distant ancient art, we can see the national foundation of art. The reason why pyramids and human-faced beasts were discovered in Egypt is because this art is a manifestation of the Egyptian national spirit. What they display is precisely the Egyptian national consciousness. The pyramid is a tomb building. Its rise is sufficient to reflect the religious beliefs of Egyptians regarding the concept of the dead. Human-faced beasts and other art forms are all expressions of Egyptian national religion. The great buildings and sculptures left by Greece are also expressions of the Greek national character. Because the Greek nation has a brave and lively spirit, a beautiful and strong body, excited and enthusiastic emotions, a demand for material enjoyment, a this-worldly thought rather than a transcendent religious view of life, and an interest in sports, what is expressed in Greek art is precisely the Greek national spirit. The Venus statue, which is most easily seen by the general public, is enough to reflect the Greek nation's religious concept symbolizing life. The more common discus thrower also clearly shows the spirit of the Greeks' love of sports. In Greek art, we see the full expression of the Greek nation. Even in the Middle Ages, in that politically unstable, medieval century filled with local feudalism and lacking national consciousness, the architecture, sculpture, and painting that were popular at the time each had its national color to some extent.

The national color of art became increasingly obvious. When the feudal system of the Middle Ages gradually collapsed, national consciousness grew more and more. The enthusiastic movement of the Renaissance, which opened the way for modern art, was its creation of national art from the constraints of medieval Gothic art. Because of it, we see that the Renaissance and the Baroque and Rococo art that followed are all manifestations of emerging national consciousness.

In literature, the national element of literature exists in the same way as art. Although we cannot now determine its original form, we can be deeply convinced that it must be based on the general consciousness of the nation. This can be clearly understood in the Iliad and Odyssey of Greece, the Nibelungenlied of Germany, the Beowulf of England, the Song of Roland of France, and the Book of Songs, Airs of the States in our country. In the West, the development of national literature must rely on the destruction of the dominance of Latin and the use of national languages. The reason why the Renaissance opened the way for modern literature is that Dante and Chaucer each worked hard to use the national language of their respective nations as a means of their literary expression. In England, due to Chaucer's efforts, we see the brilliant literary era of the Elizabethan era and later.

From these art records, we can understand the origin of literature and art 丨丨 that is, the highest mission of art is to express the national spirit and consciousness to which it belongs. In other words, the highest meaning of literature and art is nationalism.

(3)

The full development of nationalistic literature and art, on the one hand, depends on the establishment of national consciousness in politics, and on the other hand, directly affects the establishment of nationalism in politics.

Regarding the former, the full development of national literature and art must await the establishment of a national state in politics. The development of national literature and art must be accompanied by the emergence of a national state. Therefore, in modern times, we see the full development of national literature and art.

Since the Congress of Vienna in 1815, all parts of Europe have been filled with nationalistic ideas. At that time, there were no independent national states of Germany, Italy, Hungary, Poland, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and Finland on the map of Europe. Therefore, at that time, the nationalistic movement was very turbulent. The purpose of nationalism was to form independent national states. Hungary was under the iron heel of the Habsburgs, and Germany was full of the remnants of the feudal system. Under the same nation, there were many small feudal princes. "Italy is only a geographical term." The Hungarian nationalist movement of people like Szechinye was finally conquered by the Habsburgs. The Habsburg Empire was the hegemon of the European political situation at that time. Under its rule, there were many feudal princes left by the Holy Roman Empire and many political organizations of the so-called Italy. Under this situation, Prussia and Sardinia were the most active in striving for nationalism. We do not need to repeat here how they struggled. At least since the Congress of Vienna, the European nations have recognized that their only way out is nationalism. They began to run in this direction. This road is not a broad road, of course, it is exceptionally rugged.

1871 is a very memorable year. In that year, not only was France defeated miserably by Germany, but it is also memorable because of the success of the European nationalist movement. Since 1815, Germany has recognized this road of nationalism. Because there were too many small princes, Prussia had to be pushed out to be the leader of their nationalist movement. The result was the establishment of the German national state.

1871 is also worth commemorating for the emergence of the Italian nation. Although Italy already had a national state before this year, Rome was still under French occupation. The result of the Franco-Prussian War was the recall of the French troops in the occupation of Rome, allowing the national Italian state to establish its capital in Rome丨Italy's inevitable capital.

Since 1871, although the Germans and Italians have realized their national movements, the European national movement has not stopped because of this. The Balkan issue, from the Berlin Conference to the present, has never been resolved satisfactorily by all parties, and the reason for the brewing of war is the national movement there. At the same time, the Slavic nations subjugated under the Habsburgs began their political national movement after 1871. It was not until the European War after 1914丨1918 that their attempt was realized. As a result of the European War, we saw the emergence of more national states and the collapse of the two major empires. The Slavic nations under the iron heel of the Habsburgs realized their hopes. We saw the establishment of national states such as Yugoslavia and Czechoslovakia.

As a result of the Russian Revolution in November 1917, we not only saw the collapse of Romanov imperialism, but also saw more successes of nationalism at the same time. Not only have nations such as Finland, Poland, Latvia, Lithuania, and Estonia all broken free from the shackles of Russia and established independent national states, but we have also seen the Ukrainian, Belarusian, South Caucasian, Turkic, and Uzbek nations all establish autonomous national states. Even the Russian Socialist Soviet Federal Republic is composed of eleven autonomous states and twelve autonomous regions. This shows that the power of nationalism is enduring and great.

Recently, the National Revolution of China, the establishment of the Republic of Turkey, the free movement of Ireland, the independence movement of the Philippines, and the independence movements of Korea, India, and Vietnam are even more filled with records of the national movement. Therefore, modern literature and art are also filled with the nationalistic movement. Just as the way out in politics is nationalism, the way out for the development of literature and art is also concentrated on nationalism.

The first mover of modern French art was Cézanne. He combined the propositions of various schools of art popular in France at the time, such as the Impressionist focus on the phenomenon of light, Ingres' theory of the universe in painting, and Courbet's realism, and added his own original propositions 丨 the so-called self-expression and emphasis on the form of lines, evolving into the so-called later Cubism and Fauvism, and finally evolving into the so-called "Purism". In this diverse art world, the central consciousness is still one: the French national consciousness.

In Germany, the Germans have their own national art. Their movement is concentrated under the banner of Expressionism. The so-called Expressionism is the expression of the German national spirit and national consciousness. Therefore, Expressionism is particularly rich in strong national characteristics. As Professor Brinton said, "German modern art is the so-called Expressionism, full of German national characteristics."

In addition, the Italians' efforts in national art are concentrated on Futurism, and the Russians' efforts in national art are concentrated on Primitivism. These -isms are all expressions of their national spirit and national consciousness. As mentioned earlier, we can understand very well that the progress of literature and art follows the progress of politics. Therefore, the establishment of national literature and art must await the establishment of a national state.

Regarding the latter, the national movement in literature and art directly affects the establishment of nationalism in politics. This is very clear in the development of Yugoslavia. The Yugoslav national art movement preceded the birth of the Yugoslav nation-state. The Yugoslav Artists' Association, established in 1905 by Mestnovic, was the beginning of the concrete organizational activities of Yugoslav national art. They focused their expression on the historical storms and the national will of the South Slavic nation. Due to the establishment of Yugoslav national art, we saw the emergence of the Yugoslav nation-state after the European War.

Therefore, art and literature must be based on the nation. This fact cannot be denied. But what is the content contained in nationalistic literature and art?

(4)

A nation is a group of races. The formation of this group of races is determined by common cultural, historical, physical, and psychological points. The common struggle of the past is the only prerequisite for the formation of a nation. The continuous common struggle is the only prerequisite for the survival and evolution of a nation. Therefore, the purpose of nationalism is not only passively to maintain the survival of that group of races, but also to actively exert the strength of that group of people and increase the glory of that group of people.

Art and literature belong to a certain nation, are for a certain nation, and are produced by a certain nation. Their purpose is not only to express the folk thoughts, folk religions, and national sentiments of the nation to which they belong, but also to eliminate all thoughts that hinder national progress, to promote the will of national upward development, and to express the history of all struggles in the process of the nation increasing its own glory. Therefore, nationalistic literature and art not only express the already formed national consciousness, but also create the new life of the nation.

Belonging to the primary national art, expressing national sentiments, we see modern German Expressionism, Russian Primitivism, and French Purism.

Belonging to the secondary national art, we see Italian Futurism and Yugoslav modern art. The central consciousness of Futurism lies in the praise of material or mechanical civilization. We see that Italy is a country lagging behind in material civilization in the West. Precisely because of this, Futurism appeared in Italy to create the Italian nation's awareness of material civilization. Yugoslav national art, under the leadership of Ivan Mestrovic, not only expresses the past struggles of their nation, but also strives to establish the national consciousness of the people of the South Slavic nation.

(5)

The current crisis in our Chinese literary and art scene is the lack of a central consciousness of literature and art. Then, if we want to break through this crisis and promote the development of our literature and art, we must form a central consciousness of literature and art. From the lessons of history, we must concentrate our future efforts on the creation of nationalistic literature and art. Our future literary and artistic activities should be centered on awakening our national consciousness. At the same time, in order to promote the prosperity of our nation, we must promote the will of the nation to develop upward and create a new life for the nation. What we are now bearing is the important and great mission of establishing our nationalistic literature and art.

Qingfeng Garden

Sending Students to France by the College of Law and Politics 186

This good news has already been widely reported in the education news columns of the major newspapers in this city on June 18th. Now, for the sake of having a basis for this article, I will transcribe the news report as follows:

"The Shanghai College of Law and Politics (formerly Shanghai University of Law and Politics) on Jin Shenfu Road, Shanghai, since being managed by Dr. Zheng Yuxiu and Dr. Zhu Foding, has been striving to plan and develop, and is developing day by day. Recently, it has been approved and registered by the Ministry of Education of the National Government. Now, in order to cultivate talents, the school has selected five outstanding graduates from this year's graduating class to study in France, including three female students and two male students. It is planned to increase the number to ten or fifteen in the next session," which is not wrong. This is not an exaggerated publicity stunt by the College of Law and Politics. The fact is indeed so. We are so happy that the registration issue, which is of great importance to the future, has finally been approved by the Ministry of Education as a result of the efforts of Dr. Zheng and Dr. Zhu. Not only has the school been registered, but the students seem to have gained a bright future, and the authorities are also sending students to France to study, which especially gives the students special hope. However, according to the news that has been circulating, the five people sent to France this time do not need to go through the examination and selection process, but have already been decided internally by the authorities. Therefore, the students are discussing it one after another. Some say that of the 200 graduates of the College of Law and Politics this year, female students only account for two-tenths, but of those sent to France, two are male and three are female. It is not that the school authorities value women over men, but that the female students' grades are particularly superior to the male students'. Therefore, it has increased the ambition of the female students and extinguished the prestige of the male students. Some say that sending students to study abroad without organizing an examination committee to solemnly select true talents may lead to the abuse of planting private parties and violate the purpose of cultivating talents. Therefore, they cannot help but have doubts about this issue.

Moreover, the fact is like this. According to people who know the inside story, the three ladies sent to France this time are Zhang Shizhu and Zhang Cuiwu. Therefore, there are more discussions among the students. Some say that both Ms. Zhang and Ms. Zhang graduated from the specialized department of the law department this year. In terms of qualifications and knowledge, can it be that the forty or fifty undergraduates are not as good as them? Some say that whether their grades are excellent or not is not to be discussed for the time being, but because they have entered the specialized department, they do not study foreign languages according to the regulations, so they do not understand French. The school authorities do not send undergraduates who have studied French for four years according to the regulations, but prefer to send Ms. Zhang and Ms. Zhang who do not understand French, which seems to be making fun of them.

The above discussions from all sides seem to be reasonable, but they are still the views of scholars and do not fit the current situation. I think the students should not be so forgetful. In the spring of this year, a movement to expel the president occurred at the school. The situation was precarious and could not last. Fortunately, Ms. Zhang Shizhu served as the interim chairman of the students' general assembly, and Ms. Zhang Cuiwu served as the record of the general assembly. In this way, the students' forces stood against each other, and the few elements who controlled the student union were softened, and the movement to expel the president was able to pass safely. If there had been no efforts from Ms. Zhang and Ms. Zhang at that time, I am afraid that the College of Law and Politics would have long been unrecognizable, and there would be no success in registration and celebration of peace today. According to the merits and rewards, Ms. Zhang and Ms. Zhang's being sent to study abroad is well deserved. Moreover, aren't Ms. Zhang and Ms. Zhang reciting French every day, morning and night, with "A, Pan, Shuai, Tai"? (Sword)

The Yong'an Music Department announced that the company received a large number of newly released tenth-period Bige records yesterday. Among them, "The Shopkeeper and the Moon and the Green Clouds," "Cai E Bids Farewell to Fengxian by Pei Shan and Bi Yun," and "Mr. Huang Gefei, a Musician, Sighs as the Boss of Ziyue Shop" are all extremely exciting works. There are also many kinds of Collin Far East and other disc fragments, which cannot be listed in detail. They are very popular after being launched on the market.

The Sino-Western Pharmacy on Fourth Horse Road announced that the Star Flower Water Perfume invented by the main store of this pharmacy has excellent materials, elegant color and fragrance, and its quality is higher than that of the public. Therefore, the sales volume has increased sharply, which is beyond expectations. In this summer, more is needed. It is being processed and rushed day and night, and it is still feared that it will not be able to keep up. Now, in order to promote it in other places, Tang Biaonan has been specially appointed as a representative to go to the capital area to promote this perfume. According to reports from the representative, the results are very good and are warmly welcomed by the people there.

The Shanghai Gramophone Clock Company at No. 15 Zhifu Road announced that since the company's recent price reduction, customers have been crowded and the partners are overwhelmed. A large number of gold and silver clocks shipped from Europe and the United States are sold at the original price, and there is a cheap department. A new type of gramophone sells for only nine and a half yuan each, and each record sells for one yuan. The repair department hires experienced technicians to ensure accuracy, and the wages are not calculated.

Dance News 188

Dancer Kyle announced that he has opened a dance school opposite the Paris Grand Theater on Xiafei Road in the French Concession for a long time. Many Chinese ladies have gone to study. He teaches scholars with the correct posture, and the teaching method is novel and easy to understand. There are special classes and general classes, which can be learned day and night. The fees are cheap. There is also a tea dance every Sunday afternoon to help scholars' interest. Those who wish to learn social dance can come to register at any time.

Theater News 189

Tianyi Film Company announced that the company's new film "Yang Naiwu and Xiaobaicai" has been released at the Central Grand Theater. Although the weather was cloudy and rainy for the past two days, the day and night games were full half an hour before the screening. Most of those who arrived later regretted it. Today is the last day. From tomorrow, the second episode will be shown and the stage play "Yang Naiwu Second Book" will continue to be performed.

The Meihua Song and Dance Troupe announced that the members of the troupe have been performing in Wuhan since the beginning of April, and have been welcomed by the local gentlemen and ladies. They have been re-elected for more than a month. Every day and every game is announced to be full. Nearby ports such as Changsha and Yichang have heard of the name and come to hire, and have been warmly welcomed. Therefore, the scheduled central performance on the 17th cannot be held as scheduled. Recently, the troupe members received a call from Yichang, and there are also newly compiled fragrant and ideal ancient costume song and dance drama "Taixu Realm", long love song and dance "Mandarin Duck Sword", martial arts song and dance "Fighting Bull Guest", fragrant song and dance drama "Luoshen", etc. All clothing and cloth shadows cost more than 10,000 yuan.

Publishing News 190

China Business Propaganda Agency announced that Shanghai is a large port for international trade, and its prosperity is at its peak. However, the land is wide and there are many shops. Occasionally, it is difficult to remember the business aspects. Since the China Business Propaganda Agency has taken this into consideration, it has specially ordered commissioners to conduct a two-year investigation of the business community. The results obtained have been compiled into a Shanghai Commercial Directory Map, using Shepherd brand eighty-pound wood-made paper, four-color fine printing, with a diameter of four feet and three inches and a width of six feet and two inches. The content lists the city's shops and is clearly marked. Once viewed, it can be found according to the map and is clear at a glance. The company has reprinted 15,000 copies, which have been completed. Now, in order to facilitate the purchase of ordinary people, only one yuan of ocean is charged, and postage stamps are universal. The original class will be registered and sent. The head office is located at No. 31 B, East Yokohama Road, Shanghai, and the branch office is located on the second floor of No. 3040, Haining Road.
